Current Commentary

A Calm Discussion on the Rickshaw Craze 23

Since the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession issued the new regulations for rickshaw licenses, the Rickshaw Trade Association immediately threatened resistance. Recently, the craze has escalated, and the situation is severe. This matter concerns the livelihood of 140,000 common people and deserves attention. According to the Municipal Council's decision, from August onwards, those applying for rickshaw licenses must first submit the vehicle owner certificate issued by the Management Committee for verification. Before obtaining the vehicle owner certificate, they must declare their willingness to abide by the new regulations. The content of the new regulations is based on clauses 4 to 16 of the Rickshaw Committee's recommendations, which were approved by the Municipal Council Board. In summary, they are: (1) Implement vehicle owner registration as soon as possible. (2) Establish a rickshaw puller registration system. (3) Stipulate a maximum rental of 80 cents per 24 hours for public rickshaws. (4) Set fares at 20 cents per mile and 60 cents per hour. (5) Crack down on illegal chartered rickshaws. This resistance craze is mainly led by the Trade Association, organized by rickshaw owners. Upon closer inspection of the new regulations, the items most directly affecting the interests of rickshaw owners are only vehicle owner registration and the reduction of rickshaw rental fees.

Before discussing the rights and wrongs of this matter, we should first acknowledge that there is indeed a need to improve the current rickshaw system and the lives of rickshaw pullers. However, the Municipal Council and the Trade Association clearly have different approaches to improvement. According to the Municipal Council's observations, the shortcomings of the current system are mostly due to the control of licenses in the hands of a few, allowing them to monopolize the market. This leaves helpless rickshaw pullers exploited and with no recourse. It is said that since 1924, when the Municipal Council limited the number of licenses for traffic management purposes, three major drawbacks have emerged: (1) License holders have gained monopolistic value, causing rickshaw pullers to pay high rental prices. (2) The emergence of "illegal" chartered rickshaws. (3) The style of rickshaws in the Public Concession is inferior to that of other cities. Therefore, the main target of the Municipal Council's new regulations is to crack down on the illegal monopoly and sale of licenses. The Trade Association, which the Rickshaw Committee report identifies as controlling the buying and selling of licenses, is therefore the first to be affected. Conversely, the Trade Association only admits that "some rickshaw owners sell their vehicles when they change careers due to certain reasons, but there should absolutely not be any buying and selling of licenses alone." (See Mr. Yin Zhiling's speech in this newspaper on March 21st.) If this is true, then the opposition to vehicle owner registration seems to be a shot in the dark. This point is a matter of fact and cannot be forcibly concealed.

We believe that since the Trade Association and rickshaw owners in general do not admit to the buying and selling of licenses, the main reason for opposing the new regulations lies only in the reduction of rickshaw rental fees. However, based on reality, there is still room for negotiation on the issue of rent reduction. It is said that the Municipal Council initially planned to reduce the rent to 80 cents per day from July 1st, but later postponed it to August 1st and changed it to 100 cents per day. Only on January 1st of next year will it be reduced to 80 cents. This shows that the Municipal Council has not insisted on its original proposal. The Trade Association also admits that there is a need to appropriately reduce rickshaw rental fees and has submitted a letter to the Municipal Council proposing a reduction to 120 cents. This indicates that both parties feel that the current rickshaw rental fees are too high, and the difference lies in the amount of reduction, not the principle of reduction. If a way can be found to abolish the "baotou" system (subcontracting system) and have rickshaw pullers rent directly from rickshaw companies, the rickshaw companies can abide by the new regulations without difficulty, and the rickshaw pullers can also enjoy real benefits.

From this perspective, the current rickshaw craze should not have occurred. The reason why it has been brewing until now, and there is even a risk of a violent outbreak, may be that the two parties have not been able to meet with sincerity. It cannot be denied that the Municipal Council is too hasty in implementing the reform plan. As the Trade Association has stated, to abolish the "baotou" system, it is necessary to first improve the lives of rickshaw pullers and free them from the economic relationship with the "baotou." If this is not done and there is only talk of reducing rickshaw rental fees, it will not be possible to abolish the contracts between rickshaw owners and the "baotou," and rickshaw pullers may even have no rickshaws to pull, which is exactly what is expected.

In conclusion, for the sake of the livelihood of 140,000 common people and the order and stability of society, we sincerely hope that both parties will not go to extremes and will work together in a spirit of compromise to find a final solution.

Vienna is in a State of Panic; New Austrian Government Established 24

Former Minister of Education Schuschnigg Appointed as Prime Minister

Starhemberg Retains Position as Deputy Prime Minister

Christian Heimwehr Faction Equally Divided in Key Positions

Vienna: The leader of the Heimwehr demanded that the position of Prime Minister must belong to their faction. President Miklas ignored his request and announced this morning that he had entrusted the task of forming a cabinet to Schuschnigg, the former Minister of Education. Prince Starhemberg, the commander-in-chief of the Heimwehr, will remain as Deputy Prime Minister and concurrently serve as Minister of Public Security, thus expanding his power compared to before.

Last night, the police received information that the Nazi Party was preparing for a second uprising. As a result, Vienna was again placed under martial law. A high-ranking police officer told an Associated Press reporter that the national police were prepared to mobilize to prevent the events of last week from recurring in Styria and other provinces.

The leaders of the Heimwehr in various regions held a meeting last night and decided to demand that key positions such as the Prime Minister, Minister of Defense, and Minister of Public Security be held by Heimwehr figures. It is also reported that Fessl, an important member of former Chancellor Dollfuss's cabinet, also supported this proposal. This resolution has been sent to Prince Starhemberg for submission to President Miklas. The Heimwehr's resolution also stated that they did not object to Schuschnigg serving as Deputy Prime Minister.

Outside, there was much speculation about this decision by Austria's powerful figures. Some said that the Heimwehr was brewing a coup and promoting Prince Starhemberg as dictator. Others said that the Nazi Party in Vienna had received secret orders to rise again. At a time when rumors were rife, the police were striving to respond. Machine guns were densely deployed at major intersections, and public offices and government buildings were heavily guarded. Vienna was in a state of panic. However, according to a high-ranking police officer who spoke to an Associated Press reporter, this preparedness was only to prevent any unexpected events after Dollfuss's funeral.

Many members of Dollfuss's government retained their positions in the new cabinet, with only slight adjustments. The power of the new Prime Minister, Schuschnigg, is not as great as that of the late Chancellor Dollfuss. However, he will concurrently serve as Minister of Defense, Education, and Justice, with General Zehner as Deputy Minister of Defense. Deputy Prime Minister Starhemberg will concurrently serve as Minister of Public Security, a position previously held by Chancellor Dollfuss himself. Fessl, a former non-departmental cabinet member of the previous government, now serves as Minister of Interior. Waldner, the former Minister of Justice, has been transferred to the position of Minister of Foreign Affairs, which was also previously held by Dollfuss. The ministers of the other three departments remain unchanged: Stockinger as Minister of Commerce, Buresch as Minister of Finance, and Stummer as Minister of Public Welfare. The new Prime Minister, Schuschnigg, is generally recognized as a prominent monarchist with extensive experience in key positions and unparalleled political talent. He is also taciturn, resembling a university professor, and is a scholar of great learning, especially in political and economic studies. (National Telegram, 30th)

Cabinet Members Well Allocated 25

Vienna: Last night's cabinet meeting decided to appoint Dr. Schuschnigg, the 39-year-old Minister of Education and leader of the Farmers' League, as Prime Minister. Prince Starhemberg, the leader of the Heimwehr, was appointed as Deputy Prime Minister and concurrently heads the Ministry of Public Security. Therefore, Prince Starhemberg is responsible for commanding the Gendarmerie and the Auxiliary Army. The cabinet meeting lasted for eight hours before the organization of the new cabinet was finalized. Although the appointment of Dr. Schuschnigg as Prime Minister appears to be a victory for the Christian Social Party, the positions of Public Security, Foreign Affairs, and Interior are all led by Prince Starhemberg, representing the Heimwehr faction. Therefore, in reality, the victory belongs to the Heimwehr. The new Prime Minister is enthusiastic about religion and has a mild demeanor, which is not greatly resented by various opposition parties. Prince Starhemberg convened a cabinet meeting yesterday, requesting a reorganization of the cabinet to restore public confidence. Initially, it was thought that the meeting would result in Starhemberg taking power. People in the capital were deeply afraid that the Heimwehr would follow in the footsteps of the Nazi Party and cause turmoil. Therefore, the atmosphere was extremely tense, and all public offices were heavily guarded at the time. Now that the seats in the new cabinet have been properly allocated, public sentiment should gradually stabilize. (Reuters, 30th)

Vienna: After the establishment of the new "compromise cabinet," a new wave of turmoil has been avoided, and Vienna has temporarily become peaceful. Dr. Schuschnigg's appointment as Prime Minister is indeed a victory for Catholicism. However, the fact that the Heimwehr has obtained the four most important positions of Deputy Prime Minister, Public Security, Foreign Affairs, and Interior is also sufficient to be considered a victory for the Heimwehr. Prince Starhemberg, the leader of the Heimwehr, relinquished the position of Prime Minister to Schuschnigg, which is generally seen as not necessarily permanent. Fessl's joining the cabinet is considered strange by many, as it is well known that the Christian Social Party opposes him. However, because the Heimwehr strongly supported Fessl, he was able to secure an important position in the new cabinet. Prince Starhemberg originally hoped for the position of Prime Minister, but President Miklas entrusted the task of forming a cabinet to Dr. Schuschnigg. Therefore, Starhemberg compromised and took the position of Deputy Prime Minister. (Reuters, 30th)

Vienna: Except for the ongoing confrontation between the Nazi Party and government forces near Salzburg, the Nazi rebellion throughout the country has been quelled. The city of Salzburg is particularly quiet. A special concert was held today to commemorate the late Chancellor, with a large number of attendees and no unexpected incidents. (Reuters, 30th)

Zagreb: 600 Austrian Nazi Party members who fled into Yugoslav territory have been detained in a refugee camp near here. It is said that 800 comrades are still holding out in the Austrian border mountains, hiding behind rocks and treetops, shooting at Austrian troops, determined to fight to the end. (Reuters, 29th)

Vienna: According to unconfirmed reports, some members of the Nazi Party attempted to secretly enter a hospital to rescue Rintelen, the former ambassador to Italy. A nurse noticed their suspicious behavior and informed the police by phone. As a result, those attempting the rescue were arrested and imprisoned. Train traffic between Germany and Austria has now resumed, but passengers are subject to strict questioning. Germans must have special passports. Apart from trains, border traffic remains completely closed. (Reuters, 30th)

Pannetae admitted to joining the National Socialist Party and said that he had been discharged from the military by Dollfuss because of this, so he took the opportunity to vent his anger. Today was the scheduled date for the trial, but unexpectedly, he jumped from the window and committed suicide at the beginning of the trial. (National Telegram, 30th)

The United States Pays Attention to the Expansion of the Chemical Industry in Japan and Russia 30

US Navy Association Chairman Advocates Active Shipbuilding

Italian Naval Expert Arrives in London Yesterday

(Washington): The US Department of Commerce reported today that in 1933, Japan and Russia ranked first in the world in the chemical industry. In that year, Japan invested more in the construction and development of chemical manufacturing plants than in other industries, and the Soviet Union's economic plan also paid special attention to this industry. The Department of Commerce believes that the development of the chemical industry in the two countries deserves attention, because Japan's occupation of Manchuria has created a tense situation in the Far East, and both Japan and Russia clearly want to actively develop an independent chemical industry to be prepared for emergencies and no longer rely on foreign countries. (National Telegram, 29th)

(Washington): Morse took office as Chairman of the US Navy Association today and declared that President Roosevelt's policy is to make the US Navy strong enough to be the backing of US policy and to make the world respect it. Morse also said that the President's naval policy is to fully restore the US's power to maintain world peace, and the large naval plan is a guarantee of peace, not a harbinger of war. However, the delay in building 102 warships and the time required to implement the most advantageous naval plan will force the United States to participate in the 1935 naval conference as the third naval power. Britain and Japan have already reached the full extent allowed by the treaty, so they can attend the conference with confidence. Therefore, the United States should implement the shipbuilding plan as soon as possible to increase the US's voice in the naval conference. (National Telegram, 29th)

(London): Italian naval expert Piscia arrived here yesterday and will have discussions with the British Foreign Office starting tomorrow. Piscia declared: "My trip has absolutely no diplomatic nature, because before the official start of the Anglo-Italian preparatory negotiations for the 1935 naval conference, technical notes must be prepared and sent to the governments of Britain and Italy for reference. I am here to contact the British Admiralty to draft these notes." (Havas, 29th)

A Scene in the Eastern European Situation 31

Soviet Authorities Receive

Estonian Foreign Minister

(Moscow): Estonian Foreign Minister Seljamaa has been received by Kalinin, Chairman of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, with Foreign Commissar Litvinov also present. Subsequently, People's Committee Chairman Molotov hosted a banquet for Seljamaa, accompanied by government officials. Moscow Soviet Chairman Bulganin also entertained Seljamaa, accompanied by Litvinov and others. In the evening, the Estonian envoy to the Soviet Union, Tofer, hosted a reception, with Molotov and other government officials and senior officials of the Foreign Affairs Committee in attendance. Subsequently, the diplomatic corps also entertained Seljamaa. (Tass, 29th)

(Moscow): The following TASS communiqué has been released here: Estonian Foreign Minister Seljamaa, during his stay in Moscow, had several conversations with Litvinov. They discussed general issues of Soviet-Estonian relations, and expressed satisfaction with the progress of these relations and the increasing understanding and mutual trust between the two countries. When exchanging views on the international situation, they reached the following conclusion: that cooperation between the two countries in international events to consolidate peace in Eastern Europe, and their joint participation in international actions that could achieve the above-mentioned goals, would certainly produce results beneficial to the interests of both countries. They also agreed that, since both the Soviet Union and Estonia are willing to preserve stable peace, it is necessary to continue efforts to strive for peace in the current European political situation, and that it is also necessary to adopt a supportive attitude towards new problems and new proposals for stable peace that arise in this context. Based on the above points, the Estonian Foreign Minister made the following statement to Litvinov: "The Estonian government declares its supportive attitude towards the spirit of the Eastern Mutual Assistance Pact to be signed by the Soviet Union, Poland, Germany, Czechoslovakia, and the Baltic countries. However, since Estonia does not have the original text of the pact, it must reserve the right to make necessary additions when it receives the plan."

Latvian Envoy to the Soviet Union, Bilmanis, was also instructed by his government to make the following statement to Litvinov: "The Latvian government declares its supportive attitude towards the spirit of the Eastern Mutual Assistance Pact to be signed by the Soviet Union, Poland, Germany, Czechoslovakia, and the Baltic countries. However, since Latvia does not have the original text of the pact, it must reserve the right to make necessary additions when it receives the plan." (Tass, 29th)

German Interior Minister on Hitler's Policies 32

(Berlin Dispatch from the National News Agency, July 23) Since Hitler came to power in Germany, he has been actively rectifying internal affairs. To understand the details, this reporter went to the German Ministry of the Interior to meet with Minister Frick and inquire about Hitler's future major policies. The answers were as follows:

In November 1918, the German army was forced to return home by the Red Party. On the march, they were made to salute the red flags carried by the Marxist thugs. However, the achievements of the soldiers who sacrificed themselves in four and a half years of bloody battles were all in vain. Furthermore, the ideals of the German soldiers to resist oppression were almost completely wiped out. The hardworking masses were once again sacrificed for the ideals of overseas opposition scholars. Millions of German soldiers died for the benefit of insignificant people, and no one cared. This was already obvious. One of the German soldiers, Mr. Hitler, could not ignore this point. He proved that the children of the nation should have a kind of latent heroic spirit. In 1914, he already had patriotic enthusiasm, equal to the enthusiasm to resist to the end. Later, the war ended and a treaty was signed, causing the German people to lose their freedom for generations. Because of this, the people with national ideas were greatly disappointed. In the dark period of German history, Mr. Hitler felt that he should pay attention to domestic society. Recalling the world war and its final collapse, he began to build the fundamental foundation.

Mr. Hitler's fundamental difference from those opposing the republican government is that he not only opposed the republican government, but also deeply understood that there was a winning system. For the war soldiers, he imagined the glory of the past and, for the sake of lost happiness, Mr. Hitler had no scruples. However, he hated the plan to restore the old situation. Mr. Hitler already knew what the rent in the country was like before the war. Since the war, the rent has increased day by day. At that time, the sovereign of the political system had no rescue plan. Later, the war suddenly collapsed, and he immediately succumbed to the Red Party, which was enough to show the weakness of the political internal affairs department. In fact, they lost the hearts of the people when they led the army to the extreme.

Mr. Hitler knew that the source of failure should be eradicated fundamentally, and that the shortcomings of the middle-class German world philosophy should be transcended. In 1918, a movement occurred. This movement had already sprouted several years before the war. Since the empire in 1871, the speed of economic growth has been increasing. Due to the changes in the theory of equal division of land rights, it has become obvious that the country is the most industry-based in the universe. This sudden change has been indifferent to the middle class, and as a result, the tendency of pragmatism has emerged. It has not yet worn the mask of advocating free thought, but there are other skeptics, manipulators, and utilizers of liberalism, who are superficially compliant and deliberately destroy the democratic system. The middle class has gained verbal benefits, but does not know for sure what it should get. In 1918, the middle class supported the Red Party. The people of Germany knew that they would only be reactionary in the end and had no power to restore the empire. There was also a majority of the people who claimed to represent the people with property, but they were as different as horses and cows. Mr. Hitler wanted to be jointly responsible with them, but Mr. Hitler knew their desires and pain, and felt that they were treated as second- and third-class citizens. The world's property was used as a strategy for various prices. The pain of the middle class and their hypocrisy were extremely evil. German workers were driven by internal dissatisfaction and were never anesthetized by Marxism. They knew that the theory of pragmatism was rough and easy to understand, and that the external search for the enemies of capitalism had been realized externally. The national concept and national unity were invisibly eliminated and destroyed by traitors. The middle class's belief in internationalism was born from this. No country in the world believes in Marxism as much as Germany, and no other country's opposition has gained such a large volume. After Mr. Hitler incited, he had his own experience. Later, those who were jealous tried their best to advocate selfish ambition. Mr. Hitler had to abandon his work, but no one was enthusiastic about this kind of contempt for national prosperity. In the face of the enemy, he had no courage to work for socialism. From this, it can be seen that four and a half years of hard fighting were in vain, and infinite rebellion was produced in the country, that is, the collapse of the people, which was actually due to this. Moreover, the destruction of the imperial flag in the world may not be due to this. The German working class, in the eyes of millions of martyrs, seemed to be responsible, while the frontline soldiers were merely holders of various occupations who died in vain. Mr. Hitler was confident that he should have a two-pronged approach. He should revive the people with national ideas, and then the country could regain its work. No matter what kind of German, he should be as patriotic as Mr. Hitler. In the situation of party struggle, Mr. Hitler pioneered National Socialism to save the Germans living in the world. It was the beginning of the struggling commemorative day. At that time, there were combatants in the European War who were corporals and responded to Mr. Hitler. Another comrade was good at administrative affairs and was invited to advocate the doctrine created by Mr. Hitler. Even in the dark period, the concept of saving Germany stood firm and was able to come up with a wonderful plan to gather new atmosphere. The morale of the people has been increasing day by day. (To be continued)

The Relationship Between Hindenburg and Hitler is Extremely Tense 37

(Paris) The German newspaper "Paris Daily" published here stated that the relationship between German President Hindenburg and Chancellor Hitler is still extremely tense. Two regiments of the National Defense Force are currently stationed near Neudeck and are in a state of alert. Their only task is to ensure the freedom of President's personal actions. As for Prussian Prime Minister Goering, he recently seemed to propose to President Hindenburg to protect the President with his guards. The President refused, saying that the National Defense Force could be responsible for the protection. If Goering's guards marched to Neudeck, their weapons would be disarmed. At that time, anyone who dared to resist would be regarded as a traitor and arrested according to law. Seeing that the President's attitude was so firm, Goering cancelled the previous proposal. (Havas, 30th)

Opening of the Philippine Constitutional Convention 38

The United States Expresses Non-Interference

Manila Two hundred representatives met in the House of Representatives here today to draft a constitution for the Philippine Republic based on the Philippine Independence Act. The form of the constitution is a republic, so the Philippines and China will be sister republics in the Far East. And those who follow the US Congress will take the Philippines as the beginning. The constitutional convention opened at 10:00 this morning and was convened by Senate President Quezon. Quezon is the leader of the Philippine independence movement and is said to be the first president of the Philippine Republic. However, Quezon is not a representative of the constitutional convention. It was hoped that Governor-General Murphy would attend the meeting and give a speech, but this did not happen. It is said that this is an expression of the United States' unwillingness to interfere in the constitutional convention. The representatives talked loudly in the conference hall until Speaker Quezon arrived at the hospital to stop it. Quezon delivered a short speech, congratulating the constitutional convention on its greatest success. (National News Agency, 30th)

Shanxi Provincial Government Plans to Prohibit Grain Exports 68

(Taiyuan) Grain prices in various parts of Shanxi Province have soared in recent days, generally by more than one-third. The price of wheat has risen from three or four yuan per dan to six or seven yuan. The reasons are, firstly, unscrupulous merchants speculating and hoarding due to drought, and secondly, merchants from neighboring provinces purchasing and hoarding in large quantities, some holding as much as tens of thousands of dan per household. Furthermore, there is a situation of "a market exists without goods," causing widespread panic. The provincial government is planning relief measures and intends to prohibit grain exports. (30th Dispatch)

Xiamen Chamber of Commerce Petitions for Equal Treatment for Chinese and Foreign Nationals 85

Foreign Nationals Do Not Pay Taxes

Chinese Merchants' Burdens Increase Even More

Xiamen correspondence: The Xiamen General Chamber of Commerce held a meeting on the 26th, chaired by Hong Hongru, to discuss ways to rescue the declining Xiamen economy. It is often said that there are many kinds of donations and taxes in the city's commerce, and the burden on merchants is very heavy. However, foreign-owned shops mostly refuse to pay various donations and taxes. In fact, there are many Japanese and Taiwanese nationals in Xiamen, occupying an important position in the commercial field. Since foreign nationals can be tax-exempt, their burden is naturally lighter. The Donations and Taxes Bureau cannot obtain the tax from foreign nationals, so it seeks to compensate from domestic merchants, thus the burden on domestic merchants is increasing. They cannot compete with foreign nationals, and more and more people are trying to avoid taxes by becoming foreign nationals. Therefore, it was decided, "The association should petition the provincial government and the Department of Finance to ensure equal treatment for Chinese and foreign taxpayers." At the same time, since Xiamen already pays land rent, shop tax, and a police donation based on the standard of the shop tax, which are all considered land taxes, it was decided to request "the consolidation of land tax collection." The Chamber of Commerce's document to the Provincial Government and the Department of Finance is recorded below,

"Petition for a petition. Xiamen is a commercial port, the hub of southern Fujian, and the economic center of the province. The prosperity or decline of the area is closely related to the future of Fujian Province, and it is extremely important. In recent years, it has been affected by the depression in Southeast Asia, and domestic areas have suffered repeated accidents. Rural areas in southern Fujian have gone bankrupt, and the burden of excessive taxes and levies is too heavy for the people to bear, resulting in a decline in commerce and financial depletion. If we do not try to rescue it quickly, the future will be disastrous. I would like to present my humble opinion as follows: A. Chinese and foreign treatment should be equal. In Xiamen, where Chinese and foreigners live together, foreign nationals use their foreign nationality as a shield to resist the payment of various donations and taxes (such as shop tax, land rent, police donation, deed tax, business tax, etc.). Government tax revenue cannot be reduced, and those who are lost to foreign nationals are taken from Chinese nationals. The burden on Chinese merchants is becoming heavier, and it is becoming more and more difficult to maintain, and bankruptcies are frequent, while merchants of foreign nationality are tax-free and bear a lighter burden. More and more people are joining foreign nationality. If this continues, in a few years, Xiamen, although not a continuation of the Northeast, will no longer belong to us. Thinking of this makes me shiver. This is the first. B. Land tax should be collected in a consolidated manner. In Xiamen, land rent is collected for business buildings, and shop tax is also collected. The public security police donation is collected monthly according to the standard of the shop rent. All three of these are land taxes, but different agencies are established, wasting public funds, building houses on top of houses, and collecting taxes repeatedly. This not only violates the central government's principle of a unified tax system, but also violates the meaning of your excellency's efforts to relieve the people's pain by reducing and abolishing exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies. This is the second. C. Business tax should be collected in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry. Since the abolition of the Likin tax in Xiamen, business tax has been implemented. Tax authorities do not comply with the regulations of the Ministry. For example, the business tax on seafood is a disguised form of fishing tax, and the business tax on fruit is a disguised form of fruit donation. The business tax on fir wood and red material is a disguised form of fir wood and red material donation. These taxes have either been abolished by the central government or have a tax rate of no more than two per thousand. The fishing tax has been abolished by the central government. The business tax rate for the fruit, fir wood, and red material industries is set at two per thousand by the Ministry. However, the tax authorities contract it out to others, and the tax rate is more than fifty per thousand. Other business taxes are not collected in accordance with the tax rates set by the Ministry, and the Business Tax Assessment Committee is not established in accordance with the law (this association once sent a letter to the Tax Bureau to establish a Business Tax Assessment Committee, but the Tax Bureau ignored it). How can the people bear such outrageous levies? This is the third. The above are all matters of great importance to the future of the local and national government. What the heart feels is dangerous, and it is difficult to be silent. For this reason, it is appropriate to submit a document petitioning your excellency to quickly plan a rescue measure and to request investigation and implementation. The local government is fortunate, and the country is fortunate. Respectfully submitted to Chen, the Governor of Fujian Province, and Xu, the Director of the Department of Finance of Fujian Province, and Hong Hongru, the Chairman of the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce. (July 27)

Water, Drought, Hail, and Plague All Occur

Locust Control Methods Formulated by the Agricultural Experiment Station 96

Divided into three steps: controlling locust eggs, controlling nymphs, and controlling adult locusts

Beijing News: In order to eliminate locust plagues in various provinces, the Central Agricultural Experiment Station convened a locust control meeting in early June involving seven provinces: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hebei, Shandong, Henan, and Hunan, resolving various locust control measures. In order to study the distribution of locusts throughout the country, the conditions of the plagues, and prevention methods, the station specifically invited Professor Zou Zhonglin of the National Central University's College of Agriculture to be a special locust control researcher. Last week, Zou went to Shandong, Hebei, Henan, and Jiangsu provinces to investigate and research. At the same time, Ren Mingdao, a technician from the Department of Plant Pathology and Entomology of the station, and Qian Shenghao, a locust investigator, were sent to Anhui and Jiangsu provinces to investigate the locust plague conditions. It is now understood that the station has formulated methods for locust control and prevention, which are recorded below for the reference of those concerned with agricultural affairs.

Locust Egg Control Method: (1) Plowing Method: Locust eggs are laid underground at a depth of about one or two inches. They are protected by the surrounding soil and can often safely overwinter and hatch. If we remove the soil around the locust eggs, they will easily be injured and lose their vitality. Therefore, when locust eggs are found in wasteland, we can use plows to deeply till the soil and turn the egg masses to the surface. At this time, the egg masses will either dry out due to exposure to the sun, freeze to death due to ice and snow, or be seen and eaten by various birds. In addition, a portion of the egg masses will be directly destroyed by the plow and die. If locusts lay eggs on riverbanks, dikes, roadsides, etc., where plowing is not possible, hoes can be used instead of plows to turn up the soil and break up the clods, exposing the locust eggs to the air, where they will die from external climate changes and natural enemies. In areas where summer locusts lay eggs, plowing should be done quickly. If the opportunity is missed, they will easily hatch into autumn nymphs and eat our seedlings. At this time, because the weather is extremely hot, the egg masses will easily be dried out by the sun after being plowed up. (2) Egg Digging Method: In areas where locusts lay eggs, patrol for areas where the soil surface is slightly raised or full of small holes. Use a hoe or egg digger to dig up the egg masses, trying to destroy their structure so that they cannot hatch, or feed them to chickens and ducks. In addition, a "tail插" (a tool with a wooden handle and an iron head) can be used to select areas with locust eggs, insert it into the soil, and destroy the locust eggs, or a bamboo pole about one foot long and about one inch in diameter can be used, with the lower two inches or so cut diagonally into a sloping surface with a slightly pointed end. When using it, insert the pointed end of the bamboo pole next to the small hole, then turn the bamboo pole and lift it upwards to dig out the egg mass. Locust Nymph Control Method: (1) Ditch Digging Method: Digging ditches to control locust nymphs is a very effective method. When locust nymphs migrate, they move forward in swarms. We can dig ditches in front of the nymphs to block them. The length of the ditch is not fixed and can be determined based on the area covered by the nymphs. The width of the ditch should be determined based on the instar of the nymphs, because the jumping ability of nymphs of different instars is different. The larger the nymph instar, the stronger the jumping ability. The width of the ditch surface should be more than three 日餘 inches, and the depth should be about three to four feet. In this way, the two walls of the ditch will be inwardly inclined. The soil dug from the ditch should be piled in front of the migrating nymphs to prevent them from jumping over the ditch and falling into it. The ditch walls should be smooth so that the nymphs cannot crawl out after falling in. Deep pits should be dug in the ditch every five or six feet. Locust nymphs will naturally fall into the pits after jumping into the ditch. After the ditch is dug, locust control personnel should line up and surround the locust nymphs, driving them into the ditch. Then, use baskets or nets to scoop them out and bury them in pits to prevent rot. They can also be used as fertilizer in the future. (2) Encirclement and Beating Method: If locust nymphs appear in plains, wastelands, or thatch fields, they can be wiped out using the encirclement and beating method. When encircling and beating, first erect a flag in the center of the nymph area. The people beating the nymphs should each prepare a broom (made of bamboo tips or willow branches) or a specially made locust-beating broom. They should all go to the locust area and surround the nymph swarm in the middle, forming a circle. Then, use the brooms to drive the nymph swarm towards the central flag. Slowly shrink the encirclement. After the nymph swarm gathers in one place, everyone should use their brooms to beat them to death as much as possible. Or, before encircling and beating, dig a deep pit in the center of the nymph area (the depth and diameter of the pit should be able to accommodate the local nymph swarm). Then, take several reed mats, each clamped with bamboo so that they can be held with both hands. The people beating the nymphs should each hold a reed mat, surround the nymph swarm, and gradually drive them towards the center, causing the nymphs to fall into the pit. Alternatively, use stack folds used for storing grain instead of reed mats, which is also very convenient. When using them, two people should each hold one end of the stack fold and gradually shrink towards the center, forcing the nymphs to jump into the pit. After the pit is full, cover it with soil and bury it. Then change to another location and proceed in the same way. (3) Duck Pecking Method: Using ducks to peck locust nymphs is very effective. According to our previous experience, each large duck can eat two catties of locust nymphs in a day. If a thousand ducks are used to eat nymphs, they can eat two thousand catties in a day. For example, last year in the Hugel Lake area of Wujin, Jiangsu, a large number of autumn nymphs appeared and were very rampant. Duck were released along the lake to peck at them (tens of thousands of immature ducks sucked them up every day, and could eliminate about fifty "dan" of nymph swarms). After seven or eight days, the nymph swarms along the lake were all sucked up. The effectiveness of the duck pecking method is certainly great, but ducks often die easily from overeating. This should be noted. For example, this year in Longtan, Jiangning County, Jiangsu, ducks were used to peck nymphs, but because they ate too much, four or five hundred of the more than 40,000 ducks died from bloating. Therefore, when using the duck pecking method, several points should be noted in advance: First, there should be water nearby. Second, the ducks should not be fed too full. Third, the ducks should be driven into the water to swim and drink water every half hour. Fourth, give the ducks a rest. In this way, the ducks will easily digest after eating the nymphs and will not die. (4) Oil Killing Method: Petroleum oil (i.e., kerosene used for ordinary lighting) is very effective in killing locusts. If locust nymphs appear by a river or lake, we can first spray a thin layer of oil on the water surface, and then drive the nymphs into the river, causing the nymph bodies to suffocate and die from contact with the oil. When applying this method, if the river water is flowing, bamboo poles or straw piles should first be used to block the ends of the river to prevent the oil from dispersing. Also, when using the ditch digging method, fill the ditch with water and sprinkle a little petroleum oil on the water surface. Locust nymphs will die immediately after falling into the ditch and coming into contact with the oil. This method is much more effective than simply digging a ditch without filling it with water. This method should be used in places near water. (5) Net Scooping Method: When locust nymphs appear near rivers, it is common to see nymph swarms crossing the river. At this time, bamboo poles or straw piles can be used to block the nymphs around the periphery, driving them to the side near the riverbank. Because locust nymphs cannot jump in the water, we can use bamboo sieves or iron wire nets to scoop them up in the water. After scooping them out, bury them in pits. Sometimes, when locust nymphs appear on the riverbank, they can also be driven into the river by humans, and then scooped up. (6) Poison Bait Method: In places where locust nymphs have little food, poison bait can be scattered for them to eat. After they eat it, they will be poisoned and die. To make poison bait, use 30 parts of wheat bran, one part each of white arsenic (which can be replaced by domestically produced arsenic, priced at about four 角 per catty) and maltose. First, dissolve the sugar in water, then mix the wheat bran and arsenic together, pour in the sugar water, and stir evenly. Then, add clean water (about 25 parts) to moisten the wheat bran until it is like bean curd residue. If some spices (such as orange juice, lemon juice) can be added to the wheat bran, it will be even better, as this will easily make the aroma spread and attract the nymphs to eat. The spreading period should be in the morning and evening, otherwise it will easily dry out and lose its effectiveness. The amount of poison bait to use depends on the number of nymphs. About three catties per mu. The price of wheat bran is about three 分 of silver per catty, white arsenic is about seven 角 five 分 per catty, and maltose is about five 分 per catty. If 30 catties of wheat bran, one catty each of white arsenic and maltose are used to make poison bait, it will cost about one 元 seven 角 of silver, which can be used to spread over an area of seven mu, costing only two 角 four 分 of silver per mu, which is still economical. To spread the poison bait, knead the wheat bran into the shape of 餅 with your hands, and spread one 餅 every certain distance in the locust area (one 餅 should be spread within every two square feet in densely populated areas, and one 餅 should be spread within every five square feet in sparsely populated areas). However, it must be noted that the bait is poisonous, and livestock and poultry should be prohibited from entering the area. (7) Bag Collection Method: When locust nymphs appear in rice paddies and other methods cannot be used for control, locust-catching bags can be used to sweep and kill them. This method can also be used when adult locusts rest on plants in the evening and early morning and cannot fly.

Adult Locust Control Method: (1) Capture Method: Adult locusts have very strong flying ability and are not easy to control. However, when it rains, or when the temperature drops from evening to morning and dew falls, the wings of adult locusts are covered with rainwater or dew and they cannot fly, making them easiest to capture. Adult locusts mostly land in reeds, sorghum, and weeds. We can capture them when they land. The capture must gather a large group of people, carrying bamboo baskets, hemp bags, and other items, and proceed at the same time. The captured locusts should be pinched to death at any time and placed in baskets or bags. After the baskets or bags are full, bury them in pits to prevent rot. If there is no time to capture them during the day, lanterns can be lit at night and captured according to the above method. If everyone can work hard to do this, the results will definitely be great. Last year, Wujin County, Jiangsu, used money to buy adult locusts. Two brothers claimed to have captured more than 200 catties of adult locusts in the reeds in the middle of the night. This is a good example.

Yin Tong's Lost Luggage: Two Small Suitcases 110

A man claiming to be Chen Qingwen's servant

Reserved sleeping berths at the Railway Bureau

The Guowen News Agency reports that Yin Tong, the Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, returned after the Dalian Conference and immediately went to Moganshan to meet with Huang Fu to report on the conference results. He has not yet come down the mountain to Shanghai. Only Chen Qingwen, the Chief of the Traffic Department of the bureau, remained at the hotel. Yin's luggage, which was sent back from Dalian, totaled more than thirty pieces and was entrusted to the China Travel Service for transportation. Unexpectedly, at 10 PM on the 28th, a man resembling a servant came to the Railway Bureau and asked to reserve two sleeping berths, claiming to be the servant of Chief Chen Qingwen. Because Chen planned to go to Beijing, the Railway Bureau prepared two sleeping berths for him, assuming he was Chen's servant. At the same time, the China Travel Service also received a phone call stating that Chen was going to Beijing tonight and asked them to send Yin's luggage to the train for Chen Qingwen to take with him. The China Travel Service also did not suspect anything and processed the large pieces of luggage with baggage tickets to be transported to Beijing by the Railway Bureau. However, according to the Railway Bureau's regulations, the remaining two small suitcases could be carried by passengers. Therefore, they were sent to Chen Qingwen's sleeping berth. Unexpectedly, at 11 PM that night, when the train was about to depart, the so-called Chief Chen Qingwen of the Beining Railway Traffic Department never boarded the train, and the man who had reserved the berth had also left. Moreover, the whereabouts of Yin and his entourage were kept extremely secret. For a moment, it was impossible to inquire. In that instant, it was discovered that the two small suitcases placed in Chen Qingwen's sleeping berth by the China Travel Service had disappeared. Initially, it was thought that the suitcases might have been mistakenly taken by Chen Weiqing, a secretary of the Ministry of Finance, because Chen Weiqing was also taking the train to Beijing that night, and his sleeping berth was next to Chen Qingwen's. However, it was later found that Chen Weiqing had not taken the suitcases from the adjacent room. Therefore, the whereabouts of the items are currently unknown. The Railway Bureau and the China Travel Service are still investigating whether Yin's luggage was lost or stolen, and whether the man claiming to be Chen Qingwen's servant was a thief who took them. They are conducting a thorough investigation to uncover the truth.

Foreign Trade Gradually Declining 114

The International Trade Bureau released

The foreign trade situation for June

The Central News Agency reports that the International Trade Bureau released the following information yesterday regarding China's foreign trade in June and the first half of this year:

Imports and Exports Both Decline 115

In June, China's foreign trade saw a slight decline in both imports and exports compared to the previous month. Imports were 86,259,413 yuan, and exports were 49,172,796 yuan. Compared with the same period last year, the decline was even greater. Imports decreased by 23,839,473 yuan, and exports decreased by 1,030,594 yuan, with imports declining the most. Although this may seem like a good phenomenon on the surface, the reason is undoubtedly a sign of the general economic decline of the nation. The trade deficit for this month was 37,086,617 yuan. The total trade deficit for the six months of this year was 301,305,122 yuan, a decrease of 35.02 percent compared to the 474,641,566 yuan for the same period last year.

Countries of Import and Export 116

As for the countries of import and export, the United States still leads in imports, totaling 20,556,214 yuan. Japan is second, totaling 9,833,351 yuan. The United Kingdom is third, totaling 9,244,156 yuan. Germany is fourth, totaling 7,755,428 yuan. Next are Annam and British India, each with more than six million yuan. Compared with the same period last year, the United States and India have slightly increased, while Japan, the United Kingdom, and Germany have all decreased, with Annam decreasing the most. In exports, Hong Kong still leads, totaling 8,405,240 yuan. Japan is second, totaling 8,166,611 yuan. Next is the United States, totaling 7,412,547 yuan. As for the United Kingdom, it also reached 6,372,877 yuan. Germany and France, and other countries are below two million yuan. Hong Kong has slightly increased compared to the same period last year, while the United States, Japan, and the United Kingdom have all decreased, with Japan decreasing the least.

Main Import and Export Goods 117

As for the main import and export commodities, rice is the top import for this month, totaling 5062.88 gold units. Metals are second, totaling 4,102.69 gold units. Cotton is third, totaling 3,367.476 gold units. Other imports include machinery at 2,900,221 gold units, paper at 1,810,376 gold units, and cotton goods at 1,026,818 gold units. In addition, kerosene, wheat, sugar, etc., all reached more than 800,000 gold units. As for the top import for the six months of this year, it should be cotton, due to the import of American cotton. Others include metals, rice, and kerosene. Tea is the largest export, totaling 5,008,468 yuan. Egg products are second, totaling 3,725,638 yuan. Other exports include cotton yarn at 3,583,721 yuan, tung oil at 3,008,118 yuan, and leather goods at 2,047,583 yuan. Silk and peanuts are between 1.6 and 1.7 million yuan. The total export volume for the six months of this year is the largest for leather goods, followed by cotton yarn, egg products, and tea. Compared with the total export volume for the first half of last year, all goods have declined, especially raw silk, which has declined the most. Only leather goods have slightly increased.

Trade Situation in Various Ports 118

As for the ports of import and export, Shanghai is the main port for sales. Imports for this month totaled 45,595,877 yuan, accounting for 52.4 percent of the total. Exports totaled 24,476,909 yuan, accounting for 49.8 percent of the total. This shows its importance. Among other ports, Kowloon, Tianjin, and Jiaozhou are next in imports, and Guangzhou, Tianjin, Hankou, and Jiaozhou are next in exports. Compared with last month, Shanghai and Jiaozhou have decreased in both imports and exports. Tianjin's exports are slightly lower, Hankou's exports have doubled, Kowloon's imports and exports have increased, and the rest are stable.

Silver Still Has a Trade Surplus 119

Regarding the import and export of gold and silver, the total import of silver coins and raw silver for this month was 165,510 yuan, and exports reached 13,101,937 yuan, resulting in a surplus of 12,936,427 yuan. For the six months of this year, the total surplus of silver coins and raw silver was 28,764,437 yuan. The total surplus of gold coins and raw gold was 18,169,488 gold units. Although both show a decrease compared to the surplus in the same period last year, it is still not something to be optimistic about.

According to the statement from the 26th branch of this association, "There has been a drought this year (the original text has been recorded in previous newspapers, omitted), sincerely praying," etc. Foreign rice imports result in the outflow of profits every year. The result of bankrupt rural areas is due, in part, to this problem. Our government is currently planning to revitalize the countryside. Domestic rice should be maintained. The price of rice is related to the people's food. On the one hand, foreign rice imports should be prevented. On the other hand, the government must strictly investigate those who hoard and speculate and give them appropriate punishment so that the rice supply is abundant and will not be raised in price by unscrupulous merchants, affecting the livelihood of ordinary people. Japanese Residents' Rent Reduction Movement Successful 120

Treating Foreigners Well While Treating Compatriots Poorly

According to the Shanghai Japanese Daily News, since the rent reduction movement has been echoed by the Chinese side, it has been gradually effective in the area densely populated by Japanese residents on North Sichuan Road. (1) Dalu New Village changed from 65 taels to 65 yuan. (2) Culture Villa changed from 60 taels to 50 taels. (3) Xingye Lane reduced from 60 taels to 50 taels. (4) The landlord of Dongzhao Lane is willing to reduce the rent as follows: 62 taels to 53 taels, 59 yuan to 50 yuan, 56 yuan to 48 yuan, 50 yuan to 43 yuan, 44 yuan to 37 yuan. Other landlords on Douleau Road are also considering reducing rents.

The Soybean and Rice Trade Association Held an Extraordinary General Meeting Yesterday and Decided to Abandon the Purchase of Foreign Rice 121

The Social Affairs Bureau Convened a Food Meeting

Scheduled to be held at Cuixiu Hall this afternoon

The Dagong News Agency reports that the Shanghai Soybean and Rice Trade Association, due to opposition from all parties to the purchase of foreign rice and the Ministry of Finance's refusal to approve tax exemptions on imports, convened a general meeting of all members at 3 PM yesterday and decided to abandon the purchase. The food meeting convened by the Social Affairs Bureau is scheduled to be held at Cuixiu Hall today. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives 122

Hengfeng Shi Hengji, Yishun Hu Bokang, Runtaifeng Wu Bangling, Wanxingyi Yan Xiaoquan, Dade Zhu Yunchang, Changyi Chen Ziyi, Xinchang Zhu Zixiang, Tongde Chuan Changyu, Ruichangfa Fu Qian'gen, Xiechangde Jiang Zisheng, Changfengyilong Jingwen, Hongchengxing Cai Yujiong, Yutai Jiang Hongbin Daheng Yang Shaoyuan, Huiyuanfeng Wu Jiazhen, Juxingcheng Wang Tianchou, Suihe Xu Dehua, Yuanyu Shen Shangwen, Huataitai Ji Tao, Dayouheng Yan Fukang, Dacheng Zhu Xiangsheng, Yongshuntai Gu Yisheng, Jutai Li Bingkun and more than eighty people attended. Gu Xinyi presided.

Decision to Stop Purchasing 123

The chairman first reported that the motive for the previous proposal to purchase foreign rice, the approved tax exemption for imports, and the subsequent decision by the Ministry of Finance that the tax could not be reduced or exempted because it had been passed by the Legislative Yuan, as well as letters of opposition from rice industry groups from various regions, were reported. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent letters one after another, and the Miscellaneous Grain Trade Association sent a letter and received a telegram from the Changsha Chamber of Commerce, requesting that the purchase of foreign rice not be made. The proposal was discussed, and it was decided that the government could not exempt a portion of the tax on the purchase of foreign rice, so it should be abandoned for the time being. Other internal matters were also discussed. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

Food Meeting 124

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau will convene a food committee meeting at Cuixiu Hall this afternoon at 1 PM. The agenda is as follows: (1) Resolve the problem of purchasing foreign rice. (2) Suppress rice prices and determine the standard number for the highest rice price. (3) Plan methods for transporting food by water and land to regulate the people's food. Wu Xingya, the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, has already sent Zhang Binghui, the Chief of the Fourth Section, to preside over everything.

Qinghai Prince Ya Lengpile Arrived in Shanghai 125

Talking About the Inspection Experience and the Political Situation in Qinghai

The Central News Agency reports that Ya Lengpile, the Assistant State Duke of the Right Wing of Qinghai, also known as Qingzhai, is the younger brother of the leader of the 29th Banner of Qinghai. Two years ago, he was ordered to go to various parts of the country to inspect industry and commerce as a reference for the construction of the province. He arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong a few days ago and is scheduled to return to the province to report his mission within a few days. A Central News Agency reporter visited Ya at his residence yesterday and asked him about the inspection experience and the political situation in Qinghai. According to Ya's remarks,

Inspection Experience 126

Ya first talked about the inspection experience, saying that the people of the Twenty-ninth Banner, in view of the importance of Qinghai's construction, sent him to various parts of the country to inspect. He visited Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Guangdong, Guangxi, Sichuan, and other provinces, and conducted a detailed investigation of the industrial and commercial conditions in various places to serve as a reference for the future construction of Qinghai. He believes that the construction of Guangxi Province has the most vitality and is the most suitable for Qinghai to learn from. The mission has now been completed, and he plans to stay in Shanghai for a while before returning to Qinghai to report his mission. At the same time, he hopes that the industrial and commercial circles of the whole country will raise funds to invest in Qinghai. In other words, Qinghai is full of gold, and no one is picking it up, so he hopes that the people of the country will go there very much. He also hopes that all sectors will first organize inspection groups to go there for inspection.

Vast Land and Sparse Population 127

After the establishment of the Republic of China, Qinghai established the Qinghai Office Director in Xining. Later, due to the frequent incidents in Kulun and Tibet, the Mongol-Tibetan Appeasement Commissioner was added. In 1915, both positions were abolished and replaced by the Ninghai Garrison Commander, who governed the entire Qinghai region. After the establishment of the National Government, in 1928, it was ordered that the seven counties of Xining Dao in Gansu and the entire Qinghai region be designated as Qinghai Province. The province has an area of approximately 2.5 million square miles, with a distance of approximately 2,500 miles from east to west and more than 1,800 miles from north to south, as large as the four provinces of Fujian, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi. The population is only 6.195 million, less than one-tenth of the population of Sichuan Province. The largest ethnic groups are Mongol and Tibetan, followed by Han and Hui. The political, economic, educational, and other powers of the province are in the hands of the Hui people. The climate is similar to that of Hebei and Shandong provinces.

Declining Education 128

Due to historical reasons, the people of Qinghai only know the local princes in their minds, so the power of the princes is extremely great. Their culture is low, and their knowledge is shallow, so the revitalization of education is the only urgent task at present. There are now more than 50 elementary schools in the province. Xining, where the provincial capital is located, has only four middle schools and vocational schools. The province's mineral resources are the richest in the country, such as salt, gold, silver, steel, coal, kerosene, jade, lead, iron, phosphorus, etc., which have not yet been developed. Industry and commerce are also extremely immature. Industry relies only on manual weaving, and medicine is the main export in commerce. Cloth, sugar, and wine are the most imported.

Inconvenient Transportation 129

Qinghai is separated from the interior due to inconvenient transportation. Therefore, the development of Qinghai should start with transportation construction. At present, the transportation situation in the province is centered on Xining by land. (1) Starting from Xining and going east, passing through Gaolan in Gansu, crossing Liupan Mountain, and reaching Xi'an, this is the main road to the interior. (2) Starting from Xining, going southwest, crossing the mountain ranges, passing between Erling and Zhaling Lakes, and crossing the Bayan Har Mountains again, passing Yushu in the west, crossing Dangla Mountain, and reaching Lhasa in Tibet, this is the main road within the province and the main road to Tibet. (3) Starting from Xining, circling along the coast of Qinghai, passing Dulan Temple, crossing Chaidamu, going northwest, and reaching the main road to Xinjiang. (4) Crossing the Blackwater from the province to the southwest can reach Tibet, and going southeast can reach Songpan on the border of Sichuan. Along the northeast into Gansu, you can enter the Great Wall and reach Ningxia. Due south along the Yangtze River, or crossing the southern branch of the Kunlun Mountains, you can enter Xikang. There are two automobile roads. (1) The Lanhuan Automobile Road, from Lanzhou in Gansu to Huangyuan in Qinghai, is 450 miles long. This road has been completed. (2) The Xining Circular Automobile Road, starting from Xining, passing through Wuwei, Ningxia, Xiliang, Tianshui, and still ending in Xining, is 2,750 miles long. This road is still under construction. Water transportation is very inconvenient due to the uneven depth of the waterways. If dredged, water transportation will be as convenient as in the provinces south of the Yangtze River. However, it is difficult to travel by boat when the river freezes in winter. The current water transportation situation in the province is extremely simple, unlike the use of boats in the interior. From Xining to Huanglan, there are rafts along the Huang River. The post office has a general office in Xining, and each county has a branch office. The northwest connects to Dulan in the province, the southwest connects to Lhasa in Tibet, and there are many postal items to and from the interior. There is only one telegraph line, with the general office in Xining, passing through Gaolan to the provinces of the interior.

Page 10

The Shanghai Municipal Council Rickshaw Affairs Committee Hosted the Press Yesterday 130

Explaining the Purpose of the Committee

Rickshaw Owners and Pullers Still Have Many Doubts

The Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Council Rickshaw Affairs Committee rejected non-registration. The rickshaw business must be the result of the fact that rickshaws cannot have licenses. The members of the committee, Maxi, Zhu Cheng, and Wang Zhiren, gave a detailed report to reporters from various newspapers yesterday on the facilities of the Committee opposing the Rickshaw Owners Association and the licenses for rickshaws that have not been claimed after the deadline. The report of Maxi is as follows:

Purpose of Reform 131

The Chairman of the Committee, Mr. Maxi, first clarified two points: (1) The purpose of the Committee is not to make things difficult for rickshaw owners, but to improve the lives of rickshaw pullers and reform the style of rickshaws in order to develop the rickshaw business. The Committee anticipates that there may be conflicts of interest with the owners in order to achieve this goal, but the Committee will always take the development of rickshaw affairs as its mission. (2) The report that Yu Qiaqing's appointment as mediator was rejected by the Committee is absolutely not true. Mr. Yu introduced several rickshaw owners to the meeting for contact, but he himself never expressed his opinion and there was no mediation. Moreover, Mr. Yu is also a Chinese director. Working together under the organization of the Municipal Council, he is enthusiastic about social work and is respected by all sectors and colleagues. The Committee will be happy to accept any proposal from him on this matter, and there is no reason to reject it.

Consultation Process 132

(3) Mr. Maxi then reported on the consultation process with the rickshaw owners. The certificates for rickshaw owners were issued by the Municipal Council from June 1 to July 21. At that time, the rickshaw owners opposed the trade association and prevented the rickshaw owners from coming to the meeting to receive the certificates. When the deadline was reached, several rickshaw owners' leaders came to the meeting and formally requested the Committee to extend the deadline and guarantee that the rickshaw owners would apply for licenses as scheduled. The meeting accepted their request and extended the deadline to the 30th. However, one week after the extension, no rickshaw owners came to the meeting to apply for licenses. Their disregard for credibility and inconsistency are not sincere cooperation with the meeting. The significance of issuing the rickshaw owner certificate is to eliminate all kinds of malpractices in donation collection. (4) The rickshaw owners should also convey the purpose of the Committee to eliminate the rickshaw industry and help the development of trams and buses. This statement is completely contrary to the facts. The work of the Committee is based on the regulations of the Municipal Council. All its facilities are quite opposed to other businesses, because it has an impediment on the elimination of rickshaws. The general opinion is that after such a reform, rickshaws can continue to exist. (5) Some rickshaw owners have registered rickshaw pullers and limited the number to 40,000, saying that this disregards the lives of the coolies and is promoting this. All the registration regulations of the Committee are intended to give the rickshaw pullers a position in terms of personality, and the stipulation of 40,000 people is also to maintain a better life for the rickshaw pullers. There are now 10,000 rickshaws in the concession, and the distribution of 40,000 people will not affect their income.

Relief Association Matters 133

(6) Regarding the rickshaw pullers' mutual aid association, it was initiated automatically by the rickshaw pullers. Two or three months ago, many rickshaw pullers went to the Municipal Council to request the organization of a relief association. The Municipal Council believed that the rickshaw pullers' own organization could not concentrate power and was afraid that it would not achieve great results. Therefore, it was stipulated that donations would be collected at 1.5 yuan per car per month, and a committee would be elected to organize a custodial committee to manage the funds and allocate them for rickshaw pullers' livelihood, education, and health facilities. The rickshaw owners are trying to undermine it and are spreading malicious propaganda, which is not credible. They themselves are also promoting the relief of rickshaw pullers very vigorously, but why not reduce the rickshaw rent immediately? Their propaganda can only know. (7) Some rickshaw owners said that they will not be able to operate after reducing the rent according to the regulations of the Committee, but the meeting has received requests from more than 2,000 new rickshaw owners to issue about 20,000 rickshaw licenses, and said that they are willing to accept all regulations. It can be seen that the rickshaw owners can also operate after reducing the rent, and the current opposition of the rickshaw owners is obviously not credible.

License Extension 134

The Municipal Council's issuance of certificates to rickshaw owners has ended yesterday. During the period, about 45 percent (4,500 vehicles) of those who went to the bureau to receive them were calculated by vehicle. The new rickshaw licenses for August will be issued according to the certificates. The date for issuing the licenses was originally scheduled to end on August 6, but it has been extended from the 8th to the 13th due to the tax office's unprepared procedures. Those who do not donate licenses after the deadline will be prohibited from operating. The rickshaw owners stated that if this matter is not resolved immediately, they will implement a rent strike. Mr. Maxi told reporters that he hoped that this kind of dispute would not occur. Otherwise, if public security is disturbed, it will be severely punished. The rent reduction will also be implemented from the 1st of next month.

Rickshaw Owners Attitude 135

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Rickshaw Industry Association's Special Zone Office, all member cars, approved this morning to take the current rickshaw owner's certificate to the Fair Road Rickshaw Inspection Office in accordance with past practices to obtain the vehicle inspection certificate, and then go to the Donation Office to pay donations and obtain a license. If the Donation Office insists that the rickshaw owners obtain the license with the lease certificate and in accordance with the new regulations, they will unanimously refuse to obtain it. At that time, rickshaws will inevitably be without a license and unable to operate. If this issue is not resolved in the shortest possible time, from the 14th of next month, the rickshaws in the Public Concession will inevitably be completely suspended due to the lack of a business license. It is also found that the rickshaw owner certificates issued by the Municipal Council Rickshaw Affairs Committee have not been certified by the donor and announced in the newspaper, so although only more than 200 copies of the issued certificates have been issued, 181 copies of the new certificates received by the rickshaw owners have been submitted to the Rickshaw Industry Association for review. It has been found that there are as many as 35 people with incorrect names on the list of rickshaw owners registered by the association and the list registered by the Municipal Public Utility Bureau, totaling 177 vehicles. The industry association believes that the procedures for issuing rickshaw owner certificates by the Rickshaw Affairs Committee are not public, resulting in many errors, and has repeatedly requested careful handling, but has been ignored. It believes that its purpose is not to truly protect the property rights of rickshaw owners.

Carters' Public Letter 136

Yesterday, the representatives of the rickshaw pullers sent a letter to the Public Works Department, stating: "Respectfully submitted, in recent months, your bureau has devoted itself to the research of rickshaw problems and the relief of rickshaw pullers. You have spared no significant sacrifice to complete this arduous task, demonstrating your concern for the suffering of the poor, which is greatly admired. The plans you have set are centered on the interests of the rickshaw pullers. How fortunate are we to receive such generous favors, which we will never forget. However, upon reviewing the new regulations set by your bureau, there are still two points that cause concern, which we dare not ignore. We hereby list the points of concern as follows: (1) Upon investigation, your bureau is now organizing a mutual aid society to handle the relief work for rickshaw owners, with good intentions and excellent methods. However, it is also stipulated that the expenses of the society will be borne by the rickshaw pullers, ordering the rickshaw companies to collect one small silver coin from each rickshaw puller per day, totaling thirty small silver coins per month. Furthermore, a lump-sum donation is adopted, requiring rickshaw companies to pay one dollar and fifty cents in silver each month, with the remaining amount seemingly going to the rickshaw companies as compensation. It is inappropriate for the expenses of relieving rickshaw pullers to be taken from the rickshaw pullers themselves. Moreover, it is unclear what purpose is served by aiding rickshaw companies to obtain these illegal profits. This method seems to create a conflict of interest for the rickshaw pullers and gives the impression that your bureau is helping rickshaw companies to exploit them. This is our first question. (2) Upon investigation, your bureau has now set the rickshaw rental at ten small silver coins per day. We do not know whether this rental amount includes the scope of the Chinese, French, and British license agreements, or whether it is solely for the British license. If it includes all three license agreements, then has your bureau obtained the consent of the Chinese and French authorities, or have the Chinese and French authorities granted your bureau such special power? Otherwise, if it only refers to the British license, and if the Chinese and French authorities also follow suit, then wouldn't the rickshaw rental increase to thirty small silver coins? Compared to the original rickshaw rental of thirteen or fourteen small silver coins, wouldn't this be a rent increase? This is our second question. In summary, we dare not harbor small-minded suspicions. We only hope that your bureau will provide a clear explanation as soon as possible to dispel public doubts. We are extremely grateful and await your instructions. Submitted by: Zhang Shide, Wang Fugui, Chen Lucai, Xu Shao San, Gao Wanfu, Li San, Representatives of the 100,000 Rickshaw Pullers of Shanghai Municipal Public Concession."

Foreign Press Reports 137

The "Shanghai Evening Post and Mercury" reports that the executive committee of the Rickshaw Owners' Association is currently engaged in informal negotiations with the authorities of the Public Works Department. The outcome may be a compromise reached at the last hour to salvage or at least postpone the riots caused by the new rickshaw regulations. According to reliable sources, if the negotiations proceed at the current rate, the Public Works Department may formally announce within days that it will postpone the implementation of part or all of the new regulations for one month, so that both parties can continue to discuss and resolve the current disputes in a proper manner. However, the actual nature of the compromise has not been disclosed by either party. According to responsible sources, if the two parties can reach an agreement, the Public Works Department will announce it in the form of a response to the Rickshaw Owners' Association's petition. Whether the postponement of the implementation of the new regulations will be for all or part of them is still unknown. However, it is heard that the clauses regarding reducing the daily rental fee to a maximum of ten copper coins, the rickshaw owners collecting one copper coin from the rickshaw pullers per day, and the rickshaw owners paying one dollar and fifty cents in advance to the Public Works Department per rickshaw to cover the expenses of establishing a mutual aid fund will all be postponed. If an agreement cannot be reached at the last hour, 60,000 rickshaw pullers in the Public Concession will be unemployed by next Monday. The last hour is not as previously rumored on Wednesday, the day the new regulations for rickshaw licenses were to be implemented. According to rickshaw owners, the Public Works Department is withholding the issuance of new licenses for August due to the rickshaw owners' non-compliance with the new regulations. However, according to the usual practice, rickshaws can still operate on the streets of the Public Concession with July licenses until August 6th, which is next Monday morning. Although the Public Works Department may issue licenses to new rickshaw owners who declare their compliance with the new regulations, if the old rickshaw owners break with the Public Works Department, the number of rickshaws on the streets of the Public Concession will inevitably be small. This is because, as of the end of last week, there were only four new model rickshaws and a few new-style rickshaws in the concession. Moreover, new rickshaw owners cannot obtain licenses for the French Concession and the areas under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai Municipal Government. It is heard that the French Concession authorities are prepared to issue August licenses to 144 licensed rickshaw owners, and it is unlikely that the number of licenses will increase. Furthermore, the Public Works Bureau and the Finance Bureau of the Municipal Government require the seal of the Rickshaw Owners' Association to issue licenses. Therefore, even if new rickshaw owners can obtain licenses from the Public Works Department, the rickshaws still cannot operate in the French Concession and the areas under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai Municipal Government.
