Islamic Groups Bid Farewell to Hu Jiaoru's Voyage Abroad 139

Mr. Hu Jiaoru, a professor at Jinling University, advisor to the Executive Yuan, member of the Xinjiang Construction Planning Committee, and outstanding young Muslim, is being jointly funded by the central government and various Islamic public organizations to go abroad to study economic cooperation and economic geography in various countries, in order to further his education. This trip will first take him to the United States, then through countries such as England, France, Germany, Italy, and Denmark, before transferring to Russia and various Muslim countries in the Near East to inspect everything. Then he will return home via India and the islands of Southeast Asia. Mr. Hu boarded the Changxing Company's Japanese Empress ship yesterday morning. Representatives of various Islamic groups who saw him off included Ma Jinqing, Yuan Zixiang, Da Pusheng, Ha Decheng, Ma Xintian, Zong Ditang, Chuantong Xian, Wang Yi, He Enpeng, Yang Yuyun, and dozens of others.

Deputy Consul Cheng of Busan Returns Home 140

Cheng Xue, our country's deputy consul stationed in Busan, Korea, has been ordered to return home. Consul Cheng has already returned by Japanese ship Pingan Maru. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and will soon go to Beijing to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on recent developments.

Tax Affairs Department Replies to Ministry of Finance: Customs Documents in Chinese 141

The Jianghai Customs Tax Affairs Department yesterday replied to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, stating: "According to Instruction No. 1349 of the Department, a document from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce was issued by the Ministry, stating that the Shanghai Pen and Ink Industry Association proposed that the government order all customs houses in the country to implement the use of Chinese in official documents. After discussion, the general meeting believed that customs houses have been using Chinese for correspondence and announcements in recent years, or using both Chinese and Western languages together. However, tax bills and other documents still use Western languages, which merchants find most difficult. It was resolved to petition the Ministry of Finance to order all customs houses to use Chinese as the main language in all documents and request approval for implementation. Upon investigation, application forms, official announcements, and replies to merchants should all be mainly in Chinese. The internal documents, registers, books, and records of the customs house should be gradually changed to Chinese. It was ordered to comply with these instructions repeatedly in 1929. The petition states that tax bills and other documents are still mostly in Western languages, so it is ordered that all documents of the customs house be changed to Chinese in accordance with the previous order from the date of receipt of the document and reported truthfully. Having received this order, it has been found that since the order was issued in 1929 to use Chinese as the main language in application forms, official announcements, and replies to merchants, all customs offices were notified to change all application forms and documents related to merchants to Chinese. As for internal documents, registers, books, and records, they should also be gradually changed to Chinese to avoid confusion. The fourth 08 return document was prepared and requested for inspection and verification. Over the years, we have made every effort to plan and change the application documents to Chinese as much as possible. Currently, all formats are in both Chinese and English. Occasionally, there are several types of documents that, for the convenience of foreign merchants, include English notes in addition to Chinese. However, all are mainly in Chinese. As for declarations and tax bills, multiple copies are often filled out, and Chinese merchants often voluntarily use English typewriters for speed and convenience. As for filling out declarations and tax bills in Chinese, it should be at the merchants' convenience. There seems to be no difficulty in customs accepting them all. The reason for the previous order is to present the current situation in writing for your consideration. (Omitted below) Acting Inspector General of Customs, Loford."

Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau Announces Collection of Land Value Tax in Yinxiang and Pusong Districts Starting Tomorrow 142

Two-Month Deadline for Payment

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued an announcement stating: "Announcement regarding the collection of the Provisional Land Value Tax Regulations and the scope of collection, and the start date of collection in this city. These items have been successively announced and implemented by the Municipal Government. Currently, the land in the Yinxiang District, including the fifth and sixth map districts Zhang, Lai, Shu, and Cang, and the land in the Pusong District, including the first map district Di, Huang, have been assessed for land value by the Land Valuation Committee and submitted by the Land Bureau in conjunction with this bureau to the Municipal Government for approval and announcement. All land within the above-mentioned areas that has been assessed for land value shall be subject to the second installment of the 1933 land value tax at a rate of six-fifths (i.e., the tax for the five months of the second half of 1933, from August 1 to December 31). Collection will begin on August 1 of this year, with a two-month deadline for payment, ending on September 30 of this year. Those whose land is in Yinxiang District shall pay to the Municipal North Collection Office of this bureau at Datong Road, Zhabei. Those whose land is in Pusong District shall pay to the Municipal Surface Collection Office of this bureau at the intersection of Roberts Road and Binlang Road, Huxi. Those who fail to pay within the deadline shall be pursued and collected according to Article 8 of the Provisional Land Value Tax Regulations and Article 23 of the Implementation Rules, and annual interest shall be added to the amount owed, and the income from the land shall be extracted and sold for compensation according to the accumulated years, in accordance with the regulations. In addition to sending a separate notice, this announcement is hereby issued to inform all taxpayers to comply with the deadline for payment and avoid any delay that may result in punishment. If any notices have not yet been received, the location of the land, the map district number, and the address or correspondence address should be provided to the bureau within the deadline for verification and re-issuance of the duplicate notice, and no mistakes should be made. This is hereby announced."

Ministry of Railways Corrects Procedures for Handling Freight 143

Proposed Improvements

Instructions Issued to Railway Bureaus Yesterday for Compliance

The Ministry of Railways believes that there are areas in the handling of freight by various railways that need to be corrected and improved. Therefore, it has proposed improvements and issued instructions to railway bureaus for compliance yesterday. The original text is recorded below:

Ministry of Railways Instructions 144

Ministry of Railways Industry Department Instruction No. 10441 states that according to the report by Deputy Director Tan Yaozong of the Ministry's Business Department and others who inspected the Ping-Sui Railway, it was found that other railways had areas in the handling of freight procedures that needed to be corrected and improved. Therefore, a checklist is hereby copied and issued for compliance and improvement. This order is issued.

Points for Correction 145

The points that should be corrected in the handling of freight procedures are as follows: (1) In the arrival station stub of the freight bill, the arrival time is sometimes not filled in. Attention should be paid to filling it in at any time in accordance with the regulations. (2) When filling out freight bills, the detailed address columns for the consignor and consignee are too brief, often only stating the station name or "(station)" and so on, and sometimes they are even left blank. They should be filled out in detail in accordance with the regulations. (3) There is a lack of understanding of the calibration of scales and the method of using standard weights. The previous Ministry order on the use of standard weights for calibrating scales should be followed in accordance with the law. (4) The signatures of railway staff and station names on freight bills and various registers should no longer be in Western languages or Western language abbreviations. They should all be in Chinese. Those who affix seals should also affix seals in accordance with the regulations to uphold the national system and clarify responsibilities. (5) In the "method of payment of freight" column on the freight bill, the words "paid in advance" are arbitrarily written as "prepaid," "paid in cash," or "already paid." They should all be written as "paid in advance" to comply with the regulations and avoid confusion. (6) All stations with two or more small scales should be numbered together with all parts to prevent accidental misuse. (7) The station names of the departure station on the freight bill should be pre-stamped with the station name stamp to avoid temporary writing, which saves time and is clearer. (8) From now on, relevant department heads, section chiefs, and station managers of various railways should frequently contact local merchants, convene discussions at any time, and explain transportation methods and benefits, so that the responsible transportation system and other systems penetrate deeply into the private sector. This will inevitably have a remarkable effect on the development of railway transportation.

Child Dies Tragically After Falling into Boiling Water Pot 147

Playing on the Escalator and Falling Inadvertently

600,000 Red Pills Unearthed from a Drug Den Near the North Station 148

Convenient Location for Transportation

Perpetrator Zhang on the Run, Source Unknown

Shengshun Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, faces North Railway Station Road and backs onto the old platform of the Songhu branch line. At about 5:00 AM the day before yesterday, the Zhabei Fifth District Office suddenly received a tip claiming that a large-scale red pill operation was located at No. 41 Shengshun Lane, specializing in selling to various locations along the Jinghu Railway. After hearing the news, Liang Fuchu, the district chief of the office, personally led Inspector Wang Zhizhang and other police officers to secretly investigate the address. They knocked on the door and entered the house, where they saw that several floorboards in the hall had been lifted. Upon closer inspection, there was a cellar underneath. There was nothing else in it. Knowing that something was amiss, Director Liang turned to check the west wing. The door was locked. He led the inspectors to climb in through the window and saw two large rattan boxes in the room. A middle-aged woman was directing two apprentice-like people to move the two rattan boxes backward. Director Liang asked what was in the boxes, but she hesitated and did not answer. He ordered them to put them down and open the boxes. It was discovered that they were filled with thread pills, 66 packages in total, with 10,000 pills in each package, totaling 600,000 pills. The woman and her apprentices were immediately detained and taken to the Fifth District Office along with the drugs. Director Liang personally interrogated her. According to the woman, who identified herself as Zhang Yinshi, 31 years old, from Danyang, the drugs were transported from the concession and then packaged and transported by her lover, Zhang Chaogang. Zhang works as a car guard on the Jinghu Railway. The cellar in the hall was used to hide the pills. When transporting the pills, they were moved from the back door to the old platform of the Songhu branch line and then sent to the train. Because each batch of drugs that arrived could not necessarily be transported immediately, they had to wait until Zhang himself was on duty with the train before he could take them out. When asked where Zhang was hiding and the source of the drugs, she hesitated and did not answer. Director Liang believed that the case was a criminal matter and filed a document with the General Bureau yesterday along with the drugs and prisoners. At the same time, he sent a document to various district offices to pursue the main perpetrator and the drug-making operation in order to thoroughly investigate the matter. If Zhang can be arrested, the source of the drugs will not be difficult to uncover.

Resolution of Rent Reduction Dispute in Yi'an Fang 153

10% Rent Reduction Effective from June

Street Cleaning Fees Also Cancelled Simultaneously

The Yi'an Fang housing complex on Rue Bourgeat (Xupu Stone Road) in the French Concession comprises forty or fifty buildings, owned by the Chinese Yi'an Company. The leasing is managed by lawyers Ye Shaoying and Yang Linzhi. Tenants, burdened by high rents and seeking rent reductions, formed the Yi'an Fang Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation Sixth District Branch. Their request for a 30% rent reduction was unsuccessful, leading tenants to withhold rent and deposit it in a bank. The landlord sued in the Second Special District Court, resulting in a dispute that lasted for over a month. The Citizens' Federation Sixth District Branch sent representatives Tong Lvzhang and Wu Guowei to mediate. The landlord showed understanding and appointed lawyers Ye and Yang to begin negotiations. As a result of discussions, it was decided that, starting from June, the original rent would be reduced by 10%. Street cleaning fees would also be cancelled simultaneously. Court cases would be withdrawn. The French Municipal Council tax would also be reduced proportionally to the rent reduction, based on landlord reporting. The Yi'an Fang Branch convened a general meeting of over forty tenants yesterday at 8:00 PM. Executive Director Huang Weiru and others reported on the peaceful resolution process. The tenants expressed satisfaction and decided that only members would enjoy the rent reduction benefit. Non-members would continue to pay the original rent as a warning to those who hesitated. It was also decided to host a banquet to thank all parties involved. All the above proposals were unanimously approved, and the meeting adjourned after 10:00 PM.

The Result of Yu Shengfu's Autopsy 160

Death Caused by Heart Disease Triggered by Stimulation

Yu Shengfu, a Ningbo native, 46 years old, residing at 390 Siwen Lane, Huade Road, had a quarrel with his wife, Ms. Xin, over family matters at approximately 6:00 PM on the 26th of this month. They then fought each other. At that moment, one of Yu's rubber-soled shoes suddenly fell off, and Ms. Xin picked it up and threw it at Yu. Yu suddenly collapsed to the ground, unconscious. After the Yulin Road patrol station received a report, they ordered detective Pan Yunlong to investigate. Yu was rushed to the hospital, but treatment was ineffective, and he died. The body was taken to the autopsy station on Fielun Road, and Ms. Xin was taken back to the patrol station. The next morning, she was sent to the First Special Court to be prosecuted and the case was postponed. On that day, Prosecutor Guo Wei was appointed by the court's prosecutor's office, accompanied by forensic doctors Wei and Zhang and court clerk Wang Zuyi, to conduct an autopsy at the autopsy station. Since the cause of death could not be determined from the outside, forensic doctors Wei and Zhang were instructed to perform an autopsy. The forensic doctors determined that the cause of death was heart disease, triggered by stimulation at the time. The forensic doctors saw that Yu's head had slight injuries, so they also opened it to examine it, but found no damage. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo and others from the First Special Court again visited the autopsy station. The deputy chief of the patrol station reported that Ms. Yu Xin had been sent to the women's detention center. The patrol station is conducting an investigation. Guo then ruled that the deceased Yu Shengfu, male, died of heart disease. The body was handed over to his sister, Ms. Shi Xin, for coffin burial. It is understood that Yu's family only has two young children, and all family affairs are maintained by Yu Xin's sister, Shi Xin.

With No Hope for the Autumn Harvest, How Can We Survive? A Farmer Actually Committed Suicide with a Kitchen Knife 162

Zhang Fugen, a local resident, 34 years old, worked as a farmer. He currently lives at 12 Yangjia Port, south of Caohejing Town, western Shanghai. Years ago, Zhang married Ms. Zhuang from the Shijiazhaizhuang family in Meiyuan through a matchmaker. Less than two years after their marriage, Ms. Zhuang took her clothes and jewelry and eloped, and there has been no news of her for eight years. Since his wife disappeared, Fugen has been depressed, talking to himself all day long, as if suffering from a mental illness. Recently, the weather has been severely drought-stricken, and cotton and rice crops have withered, and farmland has cracked. Fugen told his old father that with such a year, how would they survive in the future? Rather than starve to death, it would be better to commit suicide. His father, Guan Quan, did not take it seriously. Unexpectedly, Fugen used a kitchen knife to slash his neck around 9:00 PM the night before last. By the time Guan Quan discovered it, Fugen had already fallen in a pool of blood. He was rushed to Shanghai Hospital in Nanshi for treatment, but he had lost too much blood, and his throat was severed, so his life was unlikely to be saved.

Chinese Institute of Engineers Encourages Engineering Experts 164

Regulations for Awarding Honorary Gold Medals

Academic groups in Europe and the United States often have regulations for awarding honorary gold medals or medals to people who have made special contributions to construction projects. This is to encourage academic experts to devote themselves to construction projects. It can improve the country and society in small ways, and create happiness for mankind in large ways. The intention is excellent, so their countries are becoming richer and stronger, and talents are emerging in large numbers. It is not that they are not good at awarding and promoting success. The Chinese Institute of Engineers, in view of this, passed a resolution last year to award honorary gold medals, which was handed over to the board of directors for implementation. The fourteenth joint meeting of the board of directors recently passed seven articles on the method of awarding honorary gold medals. Anyone who receives the honor is not limited to members of the association, in order to achieve universality, but is limited to engineers of Chinese nationality. The methods are listed below: (1) The association may award honorary gold medals to people who have made special contributions to the engineering field in accordance with these methods. (2) The association's honorary gold medals are tentatively divided into one type. (3) Recipients of honorary gold medals must be Chinese citizens, but are not limited to members of the association. (4) The standards for special contributions in engineering are as follows: (A) Invention, (1) New engineering theories, (2) Mechanical items or manufacturing methods that benefit mankind and national defense, (B) Responsible for leading large-scale projects and solving technical difficulties to achieve success. (5) Any Chinese citizen who meets the standards of both items A and B of Article 4 may be proposed in writing by more than ten members of the association. After being approved by the association, the two departments of the board of directors will hire five experts to form a committee to review it. (6) If the review result is confirmed by the board of directors to comply with the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of these methods, the association will award the honorary gold medal at the annual meeting. (7) If there are any matters not covered in these methods, the board of directors may amend them at any time.

Dong Guitao Invented Jiuwei Water 166

Can Make Drinks Last Longer

Patent Requested from the Ministry of Industry

Dong Guitao, a native of Ningbo, has been engaged in industry for many years. Three years ago, in view of the fact that soy sauce has a long history in China and is the only good thing for flavoring. After the opening of the sea, many of them are also sold abroad. Unfortunately, this thing is not durable. After a long time, it will grow white flowers, taste bad, or grow insects, which has a great impact on sales. Dong believes that foreign foods have a kind of preservative to prevent spoilage. However, there is hardly a special preservative for various foods in China, so he carefully studied and used scientific methods to refine a kind of Jiuwei Water. Not only can soy sauce not change its taste, but other liquid beverages such as local wine and Shaoxing wine will not change their taste after being put into this water. After several researches and experiments, it has been completely successful. The Datong News Agency reporter visited Dong yesterday and said that he has now been tested by the Industrial Testing Institute and requested a patent from the Ministry of Industry. At the same time, Ping Sheng Arts and Crafts Cooperative Society has been organized to manufacture this Jiuwei Water to revitalize the national soy sauce and other industries.

The Nephew Saw Wealth and Took 100,000 Yuan of Private Savings from the Old Aunt 169

Stolen Seal to Change Safe Deposit Box Privately

Used a False Name to Threaten and Prevent Xu Bi's from Coming to Shanghai

After Being Exposed, Father and Brother Returned Some of the Stolen Goods

Bi Furui Fled to Wuxi and Was Arrested

The woman, Ms. Xu, is over seventy years old. Her hometown is Shengze, Wujiang. The theft was discovered, but it was still unknown that Bi had done it, so she immediately reported it to the wife of the general tycoon Xu, known as the Fifth Madam Xu. Ms. Xu had private savings, bank stocks, pearls, diamonds, etc., worth about 100,000 yuan, all stored in safe deposit box No. 735 of the Zhongnan Bank. Ms. Xu had a nephew named Bi Furui, who was the accounting director of the Shanghai warehouse of the Beipiao Coal Mine Company. He was usually of good character, so he was deeply trusted by Ms. Xu. On July 20, 1932, Ms. Xu wanted to put jewelry into the vault, so she asked Bi to accompany her because she was old. Unexpectedly, Bi had bad intentions when he saw such valuable items. He deceived Ms. Xu because she was old and mentally weak, and took the opportunity to steal her seal. The next day, after accompanying Ms. Xu back to her hometown, he used the seal to go to the Zhongnan Bank and declared that the key to safe deposit box No. 735 was lost. He asked to open the box and change it to another box. The bank ordered him to find a shop to guarantee it. Bi found Xian Kanghua, Ningbo Road, to guarantee it. He transferred all the items from No. 735 to safe deposit box No. 1064. He then took out all the stored jewelry and stocks one after another, but Ms. Xu never knew the inside story.

In the spring of 1933, Bi learned that his aunt was coming to Shanghai to inspect the jewelry in the box. Fearing that things would be exposed, he wrote two threatening letters under a false name and sent them to Xu Bi's. The wording in the letters roughly stated that Xu Weixuan, your son, owes Yu 20,000 yuan. If it is not returned, you will be dealt with in Shanghai by considerable means. Ms. Xu was frightened when she received the letter and cancelled her plan to come to Shanghai. In the autumn of that year, she planned to come to Shanghai again, but she received two more threatening letters with bullets attached, and a young man in a suit came to Ms. Xu's house to make various threats, so she did not make the trip again. Unexpectedly, in May of this year, Ms. Xu suddenly decided to come to Shanghai. She wrote a letter to Bi Furui in advance and asked him to wait at the North Station on the 25th. Bi knew that he could no longer stop her, but remained calm and waited on time, and accompanied her to stay temporarily at the Shentai Hotel on Tianjin Road. Bi made an excuse to go out, and as soon as Bi went out, the man in the suit followed. Ms. Xu was shocked when she saw him and immediately moved to the Tongshang Hotel on Avenue Edward VII, and immediately went to the Zhongnan Bank to open the safe deposit box, only to find that her 100,000 yuan family fortune was completely missing. The case was assigned to Chief Detective Jiang Shangpei and Detective Mao Yunlong of the Concession Police to investigate.

At this time, Ms. Xu suddenly received a letter from Bi Furui, roughly admitting that he had done this, and saying that he was going to commit suicide. Bi Furui's father, Bi Yunbo (i.e., Yinbo), and Furui's brother, Yu Cheng Bingxie (i.e., Bingxie), also contacted Wang Fusheng (i.e., Fosheng), the Anhui captain of the Second District of the Jiangsu Water Provincial Public Security Team, and negotiated with Ms. Xu, willing to return 40% of the stolen goods as a settlement. Ms. Xu agreed. Wang immediately took the three members of the Bi family to Ms. Xu's residence at No. 6, Lane 60, Avenue Edward VII on the 24th of this month, and the stolen goods were part of them, including 214 bank stocks, 46 pieces of jade, 11 large colored gemstones, 6 small rubies, 4 sapphires, 211 pearls, and two gold diamond bracelets. Two gold bracelets were arrested and sent to the First Special Court by detectives Jiang and Mao. The police lawyer Jiang Baolian prosecuted him for harboring stolen goods. Because Bi Furui was on the run and had not been arrested, the news was temporarily withheld.

The detectives Jiang and Mao learned that Furui was hiding in the New World Hotel in Wuxi, under the pseudonym Wang Jimin. They took the arrest warrant from the First Special Court to Wuxi on the 26th, but he was no longer there. After learning that he had gone to Suzhou, they rushed to Liumen and arrested him. He was brought back to the police station the day before yesterday. According to his confession, after Ms. Xu reported to the police station, he took the jewelry worth more than 20,000 yuan and fled to Yingkou. Unexpectedly, he was searched by the Japanese police there, who believed that he was providing assistance to the rebel army. All the jewelry was completely confiscated. Bi was released with a certificate from the Beipiao Company in Yingkou. Seeing his father Yunbo's advertisement in the newspaper, he was called back to Shanghai, so he returned to Wuxi. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi explained the case and prosecuted him for theft under Article 337 of the Criminal Law, requesting a joint trial with the Wang Fusheng case. Questioning Bi Furui fully confessed and hired lawyers Yuan Yangan and Fan Gang to defend him. Xu Bi's also hired lawyer Zhang Yuanmei to file a civil lawsuit. Judge Zhan Liangce verified the confession and ordered that the case be rescheduled for trial. Bi Furui was remanded in custody.

The Owner of the Construction Factory Shot His Aunt and Aunt and Then Killed Himself

The Two Had an Affair Long Ago

A Sudden Quarrel Leads to a Tragedy

At about 8:00 AM yesterday morning, a bloody case occurred at the intersection of Xiaoshadu Road and Haifang Road in western Shanghai. The deceased were the uncle and aunt. The details are bizarre. The circumstances are described below:

Getting Married into the Family 170

Li Jianyun is from Nanhui County, Pudong, 35 years old, and lives at No. 810, the intersection of Xiaoshadu Road and Haifang Road in western Shanghai. He also runs the Chuntai Xieji Construction Factory. Li's wife, Ms. Lu, is also from Nanhui. Initially, Ms. Lu was extremely favored by her mother, and she did not allow her to marry, so she recruited Jianyun to marry into her family. Ms. Lu has a younger brother who married Ms. Chen, named Zhanlian, who is also from Nanhui. The couple had a good relationship. Li Jianyun saw each other early and late, and because they were a family, they were very friendly to each other.

Coveting His Aunt 171

Unexpectedly, Ms. Chen's husband suddenly died of illness in previous years. At that time, Li personally handled the funeral affairs for his brother-in-law, showing great diligence. Who knew that Li saw that his aunt, Ms. Chen, was graceful and attractive, and had bad intentions long ago. Moreover, she was a young widow. Li then tempted Ms. Chen with sweet words. Soon, Ms. Chen was indeed tempted and fell into his trap. The two were affectionate and extremely loving. Unexpectedly, the opportunity was not secret, and Li's wife, Ms. Chen, discovered it and had a big dispute with her husband and condemned him with great righteousness. However, Li turned a deaf ear and lived with Ms. Chen.

Forcing Li to Divorce 172

Ms. Lu could not think of any way to do this, so she often ridiculed and persuaded her sister-in-law. Unexpectedly, the two were deeply in love and regarded Ms. Lu as a thorn in their side. In April of this year, she came to Shanghai from Nanhui and lived in the construction factory on Xiaoshadu Road, living together like a couple. Recently, Ms. Chen believed that because Ms. Lu's relationship had not ended, there would inevitably be trouble in the future, so she often forced Jianyun to take further action to drive Ms. Lu out or implement a divorce. However, Li was reluctant to say anything because of his love for his wife, but he could not bear to disappoint his lover, so he perfunctorily dealt with the matter.

Re-Raising a Previous Proposal 173

Unexpectedly, Mr. Chen recently received a letter from his elder brother, Moquan, which specifically urged Mr. Chen to quickly marry Li Jianyun, stating that otherwise, he would inevitably regret it in the future, and so forth. Therefore, Mr. Chen once again raised the previous proposal with Jianyun, but Li still responded vaguely. Chen was dissatisfied and a major conflict arose. Yesterday morning, around 8 o'clock, Li and Chen both got up at the same time and immediately washed up in the room. Chen saw that Li looked calm, so he questioned him again about the marriage arrangements. Unexpectedly, the two had only exchanged a few words when another argument broke out, neither yielding to the other.

Man and Woman Die Together 174

Seeing that Chen became increasingly agitated, Li Jianyun, overwhelmed with anger for a moment, drew the Mauser six-inch handgun he had prepared and fired two shots at Chen in quick succession, one hitting the temple and one hitting the chest. Chen fell to the ground on the spot, bleeding profusely, and died in the bedroom. At that moment, Li's maid, seeing the mistress being shot by the master, was terrified and screamed, quickly turning around and running out to call for help. At the same time, Li, realizing that he had caused a major disaster, also raised his gun and fired a shot at his own temple, collapsing next to Chen's corpse. By the time the maid had summoned the police, both were already dead. The police were immediately notified at the Gordon Road Police Station, who dispatched detectives to investigate. A vehicle was sent to transport the bodies of the man and woman separately to the Bao Long and Guang Ren Hospitals for examination, and then to the coroner's office to await examination. Staff were also dispatched to notify the families of the deceased.

Reading Q&A 186

Issue 20

Reading News 187

Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shen Bao Circulation Library

Table of Contents

(1) A Word about Canceling Registration

(2) Talking about the "New Poetry" Creation Special Issue Lu Huo

(3) Mailing 代郵

A Word about Canceling Registration 188

Recently, we have received many letters from readers stating the reasons for not communicating for a long time; and requesting that their registration not be canceled immediately, still wanting to be our reading friends. We are very gratified by this. In some letters, there were also discussions about our attitude towards readers. Regarding this, we seem to have to say a few more words:

Our relationship with readers has always been based on common interests and unforced friendship. We are not in a school-student relationship. The bond between us is formally looser than that between a school and its students, but it is more firm in spirit. This can be explained by the facts since July.

If that is the case, why do we repeatedly urge readers who have not written for a long time, and even use cancellation of registration to urge them? Why do we still issue achievement survey forms to examine readers' achievements? Isn't this a contradiction?

No! This is not a contradiction. Although we are friends, we are not ordinary friends. We are now all willing to seriously discuss scholarship. We are not literati, discussing scholarship is not for leisure. We are all struggling for life while still wanting to acquire a little knowledge to cope with our lives. Since our friendship is so serious, it should not only be a communication of knowledge, but also a supervision of life. Therefore, all forms of supervision that we adopt for readers are based on this principle. This is one.

Second, from the perspective of our work, although we are sincerely serving others and do not need to emphasize form, we cannot do anything without scientific theory. We cannot blindly shout about reading without a plan or answer questions at will. For the sake of our work, we must make various statistics in order to thoroughly understand what we have done and whether readers have benefited from it. What were the past shortcomings and mistakes, and what should be done in the future? If there are changes in the composition of readers, we should naturally adapt to them. We really need to have a very clear understanding of readers' lives.

Third, it has now been found that there are more and more people asking "Reading Q&A". People from other cities are constantly joining the Reading Guidance Department. Their attitudes are very sincere, and we have no reason to refuse them casually. At the same time, we have limited manpower and cannot infinitely expand our work. Therefore, our only option is to cancel the registration of friends whose interest has decreased and let friends with good interest fill in. This is the actual reason for canceling registration this time.

In short: We sincerely hope that there is no need for any coercion between us and readers, but we cannot do without some necessary "forms". Because reading cannot be completely "anarchistic".

A Discussion on the "New Poetry" Special Issue 189

Lu Huo

Introducing a Book of Poetry That Everyone Can Understand

The new poetry movement in China has a history of more than ten years. However, the poems produced in these ten years are things that we cannot understand or get used to. These poems are for the appreciation of the general intellectuals, not written for us.

The previous month, this newspaper's "Reading Q&A" introduced us to a "New Poetry" folk song special issue. After reading it, I felt very fond of it, because there were no difficult or Europeanized sentences, no dizzying techniques, and the descriptions were all of lives that were closer to ours. Especially, these folk songs are very much to our taste. Therefore, I have always been looking forward to the early release of its creative special issue to meet us. Now, following the folk song special issue, this creative special issue has met us again. There are a total of thirty-six creations in this creative special issue. After reading them, I wrote some thoughts behind:

Among these works, "Obstructing Transportation" (poetic drama) and "Six Soldiers" (mass chorus poem) are worth special attention. Because these are very fresh forms, "Obstructing Transportation" is well written. It depicts the rulers' exploitation of the peasants, which is very moving. At the same time, the author's use of the boatmen's singing, "Hang yo... Hai ya..." is natural and powerful, turning it into a kind of rhythmic natural music. "Mass Chorus Poem" is very necessary, but I think "Six Soldiers" is not successful. I have called several people to sing it together, but there are many places where it cannot be sung together. It is not tense to sing, and it is difficult to understand. Many characters' words must be introduced like a play before it works. I hope they will publish more such poems in the future, and they should be more advanced and able to be sung together.

The other thirty-four poems, except for "Great Love", are all worth reading. However, looking at the whole, the expression methods are not uniform. For example, "Night Wanderer" and "I am Watching" are influenced by the Crescent School, and "Stone Crushing Girl", "Frog", "Autumn Harvest", etc. are somewhat like "modern" poems. The forms of the rest, such as "Can't Go, Brother", "Coal This Fellow", "Dike Keeper", "To Father", "Little Sanzi", "Grandpa's Cow"... are more free, and the words are more natural.

Among the long poems, I love "Coal This Fellow", "Our Fort", "To Father", "Grandpa's Cow" and "Little Sanzi" the most. They depict various lives, and see their "way" from life. They all have empty shouts, and no crazy cries. With heavy and delicate strokes, they write out the past suffering of various lives, and a kind of lingering emotion binds the hearts of readers.

Among the short poems, I love "Village Afternoon" and "Stone Crushing Girl" the most. The former vividly expresses the outline of the countryside, the past prosperity, and the current collapse in just a dozen sentences. The latter expresses the life of the stone crushing girl and the contradictions of society very well.

The poem "Frog" is very similar to "modern" poetry, and it is written too vaguely. The public cannot see the theme. The writing of "Sea Breeze" seems to be a memory, but I don't think it is consistent, not too suitable. "Great Love" is a romantic technique of Guo Moruo's era, and it is not harmonious with the whole book of poems.

However, in any case, we must admit that "New Poetry" is the only rare flower in the Chinese poetry world. It is a poetry that dares to get rid of all the old shells and create songs for the public to listen to. I dare to introduce this book to friends who are not intellectuals.

This is our own poetry that we can understand!

Postal 代行 190

To Messrs. Yuan Wenlan, Jiang Ziyu, and Cheng Guoping: Please indicate your recent communication address for a reply.

Chunqiu

Records of the Fragrant Imperial Incense 191

—Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Apart from the special vehicles I have already mentioned above, the remaining vehicles are where the eunuchs live. However, because there are many people and few vehicles, they are squeezed so densely that there is no space left. It's almost as if they are about to pile up. Although I haven't visited often, I don't know how they live. However, I imagine that their situation must be not much different from the sardines packed in those flat cans.

In China, there is no name for "sardines", but since I have thought of this interesting analogy, I certainly can't help but publish it. So I finally said to a eunuch:

"You people are squeezed into those vehicles, just like small fish!" Then, I explained to him in detail how foreigners pack sardines into those flat cans. After listening, he couldn't help but laugh. So my release of this word was immediately spread by him. One person told ten, ten people told a hundred. In no time, all the eunuchs knew! Of course, it couldn't be hidden from Li Lianying! But Li Lianying didn't live with them anyway. He also had a special vehicle. My words were certainly not sarcastic to him, so he certainly couldn't be angry! But the other eunuchs might not be happy to be called small fish by others, right?

In Beijing, people have a very common nickname for eunuchs, called "雄雞兒" (male chicks), because the voices of those eunuchs are always very sharp and high, just like the sound of a rooster crowing. So everyone agrees that this nickname is very appropriate. I think the eunuchs themselves are willing to accept it, because "雄雞" (rooster) is always better than "小漁" (small fish).

Readers, imagine: a thousand eunuchs, each wearing a full set of uniforms, but the few vehicles they occupy can only accommodate four hundred people. Can you endure such a comfortable life? (94)

The Way to Propose 192

— Mu Yin

Proposing is an art. You can't be stupid. You have to be smart and adapt to the situation.

For example, if you and she go swimming together, you can create your opportunity in the pool, grab her, and say to her in a traceless way: "I always wanted to find a background to propose to you. Do you think this background is good?" Give her a surprise. If she agrees, and she is a naughty girl, she will ask: "What background?" Then she will smile and swim away. At that time, you can chase after her, grab her again, and the problem will be solved.

Aren't there many opportunities like this?

Just make sure you speak tactfully and clearly, so that she can hear your words and understand your meaning. If she pretends to be confused at that time, you don't have to repeat your explanation. It's obvious that you still won't get her permission if you say it again. I remember a gentleman who lost an opportunity because he spoke vaguely. He said to a lady, "I love you." The lady said, "Thank you." The gentleman thought the lady refused. The lady was waiting for the gentleman to make a further request, preparing to agree, but she didn't wait. So this matter passed. Later, the lady had another lover. This gentleman went to see that lover, wanting to ask him to give way. Begging is not allowed in anything, let alone in the arena of love between men and women. This gentleman's failure is naturally expected.

Also, people generally think that proposing is a man proposing to a woman. Many clever ladies are secretly laughing at this. She designed a situation for you, but you don't know. You easily let it down? Some know it but don't use it, thinking that they will maintain the status quo for a while, waiting for a more mature period. The former is stupid, needless to say. The latter is also stupid, because what she gives you after that is gradual indifference, or even sudden disgust. Friend? It's definitely not the more mature period you imagined, right?

Thousand Mile Blind Man 193

— Yan Bophong

Thousand Mile Blind Man is a famous rogue lawyer in our county (Changxing). In lawsuits within a thousand miles, once he takes on the case, there is no one who does not win. There are two things that can prove his ability is good!

One day, near the end of the year, he was returning to Changxing from Huzhou. In the boat, the boatman kept complaining to him. He asked the boatman if he needed money. If he needed money, when the boat passed Hongxing Bridge, he should crash into the waterside pavilion of a rich family! The boatman agreed repeatedly. When they arrived at Hongxing Bridge, he really crashed into the waterside pavilion of a certain family and broke the pillars. This family argued with the boatman. Thousand Mile Blind Man walked to the bow of the boat, slapped the boatman in the face, and scolded, "You are really bastard, did you shake the boat into someone's house? Can't you see me, Thousand Mile Blind Man? Today, please send him to the county." This family, intimidated by the reputation of Thousand Mile Blind Man, and knowing that they were guilty of privately occupying the official river, instead gave two hundred yuan to the boatman as the cost of repairing the boat.

When a certain county magistrate took office, he heard of the bad name of Thousand Mile Blind Man and framed him with stolen goods, arresting him. Thousand Mile Blind Man hid himself in a sack and ordered his family to carry him into the county hall. He asked the thief, "I, Thousand Mile Blind Man, have no grievances with you in this life, and no enemies in the previous life. Why do you say that I am sharing stolen goods on the spot? But do you know if I have pockmarks on my face? Do I have a beard?" The thief stared blankly and could not answer. He realized his conscience and said that the county magistrate had bought the thief to frame the good." The county magistrate was stunned. In a few days, the county magistrate was sued by Thousand Mile Blind Man and thrown into prison.

Lotus Fragrance Phoenix Tail Tea 194

— Xiong Yu

A certain magnate is known for his poetry and painting skills, and is very frugal in his self-support. He does not wear fur in winter or silk in summer, eats no heavy flavors, lives in seclusion, and hardly asks or hears about worldly affairs. Only addicted to tea, three cups a day, without interruption. There is a maid named Qingxiang who, in addition to miscellaneous chores, specializes in this matter, never relying on others. According to her, she has never drunk tea made by others in her life, which shows how exquisite his tea drinking is. What the magnate likes are Longjing and Phoenix Tail. As for the storage of tea leaves, the suitability of cooking, and the antiquity of the teapot, he does have a unique approach. Most of the teapots he collects are made of purple clay, in various shapes and sizes. The three commonly used ones are all Mansheng pots. He uses them in the morning and evening without any confusion, and specifically names them Morning Pot, Middle Pot, and the pot he drinks before going to sleep is not called Evening Pot or Night Pot, but Dream Pot. One day, a monk came from Putuo Mountain and gave him two tubes of genuine Phoenix Tail tea. At that time, the lotus flowers in the courtyard were in full bloom. The magnate immediately took a pinch of Phoenix Tail and placed it in the flower, tying it lightly. He took it out the next morning, and it was fragrant and timeless, with a special flavor. On this day, Qingxiang was ill, so he ordered an old woman to brew it according to the method. Soon, she brought the pot in. The magnate opened the lid of the pot and immediately realized something. He said, "The old maid is ignorant and secretly sipped my Lotus Fragrance Phoenix Tail Tea!" He immediately called her over and scolded her again and again, but the old woman swore not to admit it. The magnate said, "I have been drinking tea all my life and know it well. When tea is first brewed, its leaves float and sink, and the state is chaotic. This can be used to measure it, and it never fails. But this tea is not like that. Look at the leaves in the pot. Their tips are all facing the spout. It's okay to tilt it slightly, but now you have secretly sipped it all up! What else can you say?" The old woman blushed and retreated.

The Terror of Economic Aggression! 195

— Shiying

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 196

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Thirty-Two: The Generals Enjoy Themselves with Pleasure All Day Long, and the Old and Young Cry, How Many Soldiers Return?

He used to read newspapers and didn't pay attention to national affairs. Today, he suddenly felt that this important news was the text he was most concerned about. This small newspaper simply said that the enemy attacked Ping'an Fort the night before yesterday with three kinds of weapons: airplanes, artillery, and tanks. The national army defending the fort resisted desperately, but later ran out of ammunition and had no reinforcements, so the fort fell. As for the whereabouts of the army, it is not known. But are Zhao Ziqiang and his men the ones who died defending the city? I don't even know. So, besides reading this small newspaper, he continued to pick up the second newspaper to read. When he saw the third copy, it was a large newspaper. The large newspaper simply printed the three characters "Ping'an Fort" in a particularly large font. The content generally said that the enemy attacked fiercely, and the national army defended desperately. Battalion Commander Bao Fang died with the city. Although this battle was completely annihilated, it won back a lot of honor for the Northeast Army. The Northeast Army should encourage themselves. Gui Zhi didn't understand these classical Chinese very well, but he guessed that it was definitely not good news. He was now anxious to know the truth of the matter, and he could no longer hide it from the old man. So he took a large stack of newspapers and walked to the door of Zhao Weng's room, first calling out "Dad". Zhao Weng trembled for a long time before answering, "Come in." When Gui Zhi walked in, he saw Zhao Weng with one hand resting on the table, pressing on a newspaper, and the other hand pinching a dry towel, rubbing his eyes all the time. Even though he was rubbing like that, the tears still kept rolling down. Obviously, this old man had also received this bad news. He was stunned for a moment, standing and looking at Zhao Weng, he said, "Dad, have you seen the newspaper too?" Zhao Weng shook his head twice, then nodded twice, and said, "This...this is nothing, soldiers, that's what they should do." As he spoke, his throat couldn't help choking, unable to say anything further. Gui Zhi didn't need to ask what the news was. Seeing the old man's appearance, tears were already hanging on both sides of his face like a string of beads. He leaned against the door of the room involuntarily, and kept sobbing. (445)

Bernard Shaw and Money 197

— (Tao Ran)

"I don't know what benefits movies can give me, except money. Money is useful to people like me, because I am already seventy-eight years old." The world's great writer, the playful old man, Bernard Shaw, these words are really humorous.

Originally, in this world, besides money, what else is worth savoring? Why only movies, why only for a seventy-eight-year-old man?

Fortunately, Bernard Shaw was not born in China, so he can still have a fixed amount of income to allocate, handle, and for retirement. But what about in China?

Chinese writers have never been worth money. Chinese writers who wield pens can hardly even afford the minimum living expenses!

If you don't believe it, why did the suicides of Zhu Xiang and Zhang Baiyi happen one after another?

Little Common Sense

The Key to Washing Your Face 198

— Bingyu

Water is an indispensable element for skin hygiene, but what kind of water is most suitable for washing your face, and what kind of water should be used by what kind of people, are all different. Water has the distinction between hard water and soft water. Any water containing lime salt, Magnusium salt, etc. is called hard water. If you use this water to wash the face of someone with unhealthy skin, it will often be stimulated and the skin will become rougher. (Well water can also be hard water.) Even if you use soap, it will not be effective. Hard water can be turned into soft water by boiling it, adding some boric acid, borax, or adding some Glycerin.

The number of times you wash your face cannot be fixed. Often, due to occupational reasons, some people wash it more than ten times a day. Usually, you wash it three times after each meal or once before going to bed. For beauty, it is advisable to use cold water to wash your face. There is an old saying: washing your face with cold water can maintain a youthful appearance even in old age. However, both cold water and warm water have the power to remove fat. It is advisable to wash with warm water for skin with a lot of fat or people with acne. Also, for parts that often sweat and have a lot of fat, the genitals of people with diabetes, kidney disease, and urinary tract diseases, the armpits of people with body odor, and the anus of people with hemorrhoids, you should wash them more often every day. If there is secretion, you can mix half zinc oxide and half talcum powder. After washing, apply it to each part. People with anemia and soft skin should not wash their faces with cold water. People with skin diseases such as eczema and impetigo should not wash too much, because people with eczema generally have weak skin. If they have acute inflammation, the skin will be red, swollen, and eroded. Even if scabs form, it will be very itchy. At this time, hard water should be avoided. For skin diseases caused by Staphylococcus aureus (or chain-like Streptococcus) in impetigo, if you are not careful when washing your face, it will spread to the entire face. For people with unhealthy skin, after washing your face, you should gently rub it with a dry cloth. If you use soap, whether it contains free Alkali can be determined by tasting the soap with the tip of your tongue. If the tip of your tongue feels very irritating and numb, it is determined to be a bad product. However, even if the quality of the soap is good, you should pay attention to whether it is suitable for our skin. If it is very irritating to the skin, you should not use it again. Before soap was invented, rice bran was used as a facial cleanser. Today, the medical community also considers it effective. For example, it is very suitable to use a pinch of rice bran soaked in hot water to wash the face (sewn in a cloth bag) for skin with acne and other red swelling. After washing, you should wash off the rice bran residue and not leave it on the skin to avoid subcutaneous effects. If you are traveling outside and can't find suitable soft water, never wash your face. If you can't wash your face with water due to illness, then use Cooling Cream or alcohol (half alcohol and half water) and gently wipe off the dirt on your face with medicinal cotton (be careful not to get it in your eyes). After washing, wipe off the smell of alcohol with a towel. I usually wash my face with boric acid. It can prevent skin diseases, and it is especially beneficial to wash the eyes, mouth, and nose with boric acid water. Moreover, boric acid is very cheap, less than two cents per pound, which can be used for twenty days. Especially in the morning or before going to bed, washing the mouth with boric acid can prevent throat diseases and infectious diseases. It is cheap and good. You may want to try it.

Scenes from the Opening of the Nanchang Water Sports 202

Jiangxi People's Eyes Are Not Satisfied

Locals All Shout "It's Not Worth It"

(Nanchang Correspondence) The long-awaited water sports meet initiated by the New Life Club was held today at 1 PM at the swimming pool outside the department. At the same time, the opening ceremony of the swimming pool was also held. People in Nanchang, shocked by the name of Yang Xiuqiong, even though the sun was scorching, the edge of the swimming pool was crowded with people, craning their necks and looking forward with great enthusiasm. The conference period is set for three days, and the ticket price is four dimes. Today is the first day. The reporter also bought a ticket to enter the venue this year, so I picked up some scenes and recorded them as left.

A Glimpse Inside and Outside the Venue 203

A shed platform is set up in the venue, divided into command platform, guest platform, news reporter platform, rescue platform, music platform, etc., connected from left to right. As for the men's and women's dressing rooms and the athletes' rooms, they are arranged in a corner under the platform. The river bank and the waterfront are for citizens to visit. The ticket office is located inside the first gate of the venue. The swimming pool is marked in a corner of the Gan River, about 50 meters from the shore. The diving platform is about 25 meters high and divided into three levels, also built in the water. Inside and outside the venue, there are social scouts, police, etc. to maintain order, military police to suppress, and many white cloth New Life slogans are hung, such as "Visitors, please walk one by one", etc.

Ms. Yang Xiuqiong Gives Awards 204

The Sound of Orioles and Swallows on the Stage 205

The organizer did not have corresponding restrictions on guests in advance, so the temporary stage was occupied by wives and ladies. The command platform, the guest platform, and even the music platform, all turned into the sound of orioles and swallows, like a women's guest platform. Although the organizer later issued various warnings through the loudspeaker to ask them to leave the stage, it was ineffective.

Liu Xiangxiu First in Total Points in the Women's Group 206

Preparing to Shout Again and Again 207

The conference was originally scheduled to be held at 1 PM, so the audience gathered around 12 noon. It was postponed to 2 PM and had not yet started. Someone holding a loudspeaker standing on the highest level of the diving platform repeatedly shouted "Prepare to start the meeting now", but the meeting did not start until 2:30 PM for the third time. It is said that the New Life is new on land but not necessarily new on water.

Closing Ceremony 208

Temporary Moving of Auditorium 209

The auditorium was originally set on the command platform, but because the platform was too crowded with guests, the platform could not bear the weight. At that time, the meeting was about to begin, and suddenly there was a loud noise, and there was a tendency to collapse. The mermaid was squeezed in the middle and was shocked. The auditorium was temporarily moved to the stage.

Father and Son Driving Backwards 210

In the middle of the competition, Yang Zhijie's younger brother first performed driving backwards for 25 meters. At that time, his father also automatically joined the driving backwards outside the venue, like a father and son competing in doubles.

Shouting It's Not Worth It 211

The reason why today's conference audience is so crowded is because of the call of the mermaid alone. If the local athletes compete, there is no excitement, which is in the intention. Unexpectedly, the Yang sisters' performances were only 50-meter prone swimming and breaststroke. Finally, only the mermaid alone performed 50-meter backstroke, which was very brief. When the announcer shouted "Ms. Yang's performance program is over today", the audience left the venue one after another. The local old timers, feeling that their eyes were not satisfied, shouted "It's not worth it" and left.

Guangdong Ping Pong Team Wins Championship Shield for Striving 216

Captain Xu Hosts Banquet to Celebrate Victory Today

After months of intense competition, the Guangdong and Youjia teams remained undefeated, thus gaining the right to compete for the shield in the final. The final was held last night at the Central Auditorium near Yokohama Bridge, attracting over a thousand spectators. Both teams fielded their best players, resulting in a tense and exciting match that drew constant applause from the audience. After more than three hours of competition, the Guangdong team ultimately emerged victorious, defeating Youjia with a score of four to three and winning the championship. It is reported that Xu Chongye, the captain of the Guangdong team, will host a banquet at the Guanzhen Restaurant on Wuchang Road today to reward all the players for their hard work and dedication.

Ministry of Education Reforms Four Shanxi Schools 218

National Normal, Sixth Normal, and Third Women's Normal Ordered to Become Vocational Schools

Law and Education Colleges Ordered to Merge into Shanxi University

(Taiyuan Correspondence) Recently, a restructuring plan has suddenly emerged in educational circles in Bingyuan. One aspect is the order from the Ministry of Education for the National Normal School in the provincial capital, the Sixth Normal School in Linfen, and the Third Women's Normal School in Daixian to be converted into vocational schools. The other aspect is the order for the Law College and the Education College in the provincial capital to be merged into Shanxi University. The Education Department has followed the Ministry's orders and is implementing these plans separately. Details are as follows:

Two Instructions from the Ministry of Education: (1) The expenses of Shanxi Normal Schools are excessively high, and the number of graduates exceeds the demand. Starting from the 23rd year, the National Normal School should cease enrollment and be converted into a vocational school. The nature of its departments should be based on local needs. (2) The number of classes and students at the Shanxi Provincial Sixth Normal School and the Third Women's Normal School are both scarce. Starting from the 23rd year, they should cease operations and be converted into vocational schools. Their existing students should be merged into other equivalent schools. After receiving the order, the Education Department immediately prepared a document and submitted it to the Provincial Government for review and record. 219

Instructions from the Provincial Government 220

The Provincial Government believes that since the Ministry of Education has issued an order, it should be followed. Moreover, the province is currently in a period of construction, and there is a shortage of talent in various industries. The existing vocational schools seem too few. In addition to finding ways to improve the existing vocational schools, a resolution was passed at a provincial government meeting instructing the Education Department to properly implement the Ministry of Education's instructions starting from the 23rd year.

Implementation by the Education Department 221

After receiving the clear orders from the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government, the Education Department, in addition to drafting a general plan for the conversion and submitting it to the Ministry for approval, also separately notified the Sixth Normal School in Linfen, the Third Women's Normal School in Daixian, and the National Normal School in the city to implement the Ministry's orders. Furthermore, considering that the subjects and nature of vocational schools are crucial to the future of provincial construction, the Education Department specially requested the Provincial Government to forward a request to the Provincial Government Design Committee to review and determine the subjects to be offered by the National Normal, Sixth Normal, Third Women's Normal, and the First, Second, and Third Vocational Schools for this year based on local needs.

Committee Discusses Subjects 222

After receiving the Education Department's document forwarded by the Provincial Government, Yan, the Chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government Design Committee, immediately appointed Ji Zequan, the Director of the Education Department, Yu Ping, the Director of the Finance Department, Wang Qian, the Secretary-General of the Provincial Government, and Yang Sicheng, the Director of the Design Office, to jointly study the subjects to be taught in each vocational school and grade this year, in accordance with the curriculum standards for vocational schools promulgated by the Ministry and taking into account the needs of various localities in the city. Wang Ping was instructed to be responsible for convening the meeting. These officials have held several meetings at the Finance Department, and it is reported that a general decision has been made. After submitting it to Yan for approval, the Provincial Government will be instructed to forward it to the Education Department for implementation. The Education Department is currently actively planning the conversion.

The Question of Merging the Law and Education Colleges 223

Recently, rumors of merging the Law and Education Colleges into Shanxi University have been rampant. This reporter believes that this matter is of great importance to higher education in Shanxi and is eager to know the details. Therefore, this reporter visited President Feng Lun of the Law College at the Law College at around 8:00 AM yesterday (the 23rd). The reporter asked about the rumors of merging the Law and Education Colleges into Shanxi University, which have been circulating widely. Could you tell me about the progress? Feng smiled and replied to the reporter, "The Ministry of Education has long intended to merge the Law and Education Colleges into Shanxi University, but the specific merger plan has not yet been finalized. I don't know much about the situation at the Education College. I will only discuss the situation at our college. I am the president, and due to financial constraints, everything is very difficult. I am eager to resign and make way for someone more capable. I have previously submitted my resignation, but it has not been approved. In addition, my colleagues at the college are willing to reduce their salaries to maintain the college, so I have to reluctantly continue. However, it is difficult for a clever woman to cook without rice. I am very happy to hear about the merger. I have repeatedly discussed the matter with Director Ji and President Wang of Shanxi University, but no results have been obtained so far. However, it must be realized sooner or later. This matter will be further negotiated after Director Ji returns to Bing, otherwise, enrollment this year will still be a problem."

Premier Wang's Reply to the Representatives of Vocational Movement in Beiping 224

Responsible for Answering Three Points

(1) Student Employment Advisory Office Decided to Be Established

(2) Investigate the Number of Unemployed Graduates

(3) Consult with the Examination Yuan to Hold Examinations

(Nanjing, 30th Dispatch) Tan Poqian, the representative of the Vocational Movement in Beiping staying in Nanjing, was invited by Premier Wang to the Executive Yuan on the 30th. After Tan first stated his wishes, Wang replied, "I sympathize with the fact that university students are unable to find employment and have organized the Great Alliance of Vocational Movements. I am responsible for answering three points: (1) The National Economic Commission and the Ministry of Education established the National Student Employment Advisory Office last month, but it was suspended due to financial reasons. Now, regardless of whether there are funds, preparations will be made for its establishment next month. If the association cannot be established, the Executive Yuan will establish a National Student Employment Advisory Office to investigate the talent needs in various regions, so that talent can be used to its full potential. (2) Investigate the number of unemployed graduates from various universities and make an overall plan. (3) Consult with the Examination Yuan to hold examinations so that those with expertise will not have no opportunity to serve the country and society." His words were very sincere.

Yunnan Adds More Than Thirty Schools and Asks the Ministry of Education to Allocate 120,000 Yuan Annually 225

Excessive Costs Cannot Be Met

(Nanjing, 30th Dispatch) Gong Zizhi, the Director of the Yunnan Education Department, came to Nanjing and presented to the Ministry of Education a plan to establish a school in each of the more than thirty counties in Yunnan, according to the degree of need, with varying levels. The estimated cost is 10,000 yuan per month, or 120,000 yuan per year. Wang Shijie, the Minister of Education, said that the costs are excessive, and the government may not be able to allocate the full amount. If the funds were to be allocated from the Ministry of Education's original border education funds, these funds have not yet been received and cannot be used. Therefore, this matter will be discussed and another method will be devised.

Graduates of the school are always at the top of their class. From now on, the school will work harder and strive forward, focusing on the development of new life and physical education classes. Recently, in addition to the students of the Chinese Language Department of Osaka, the Chinese Travel Group of Chiayi Middle School in Taiwan, a group of twenty-two people led by teacher Shiozaki Noboru of the school, arrived in Shanghai on the Changsha Maru of the Osaka Merchant Shipping Company. After landing and resting briefly at the Tatsumi Ryokan, they rented several horse-drawn carriages and visited important areas of the city. New Development of Shanghai Japanese Correspondence School 238

Since moving to the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Avenue Amiral Foch, the Shanghai Japanese Correspondence School has greatly expanded. Many more professors have also been hired to grade papers. Therefore, the homework done by the students is not accumulated. After receiving it, it is immediately corrected and returned. This has already been praised by the general student body. The pronunciation notes in the elementary class use three types of phonetic symbols so that people from all over the world do not have problems with pronunciation, which is the most difficult thing for beginners to read Japanese. The explanation of the grammar in the text is detailed, especially in other matters. Therefore, after completing the elementary class, it is possible to read ordinary Japanese books and newspapers. The advanced class studies literary works and advanced grammar. If the advanced class work can be completed, then any Japanese books and newspapers can be understood at a glance. It is reported that the school is constantly enrolling students, and detailed rules can be sent by mail upon request.

Financial News: Silver Prices and Exchange Rates Rise, Gold Falls by Four Yuan 239

Spot Goods Arriving Amount to Approximately 10,000 Taels

Swap Discount Falls to One Yuan

After the gold market suddenly rallied at noon on Saturday of last week, the shorts seemed to waver. However, overseas silver markets rose, and yesterday's situation was difficult to sustain. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets saw increases in England and stability in the US. The Far East Gold Exchange was closed for forward silver prices. London raw gold remained unchanged, exchange rates rose slightly, US cotton rose seven points, and US wheat rose two and seven-eighths points. Public sentiment reversed, and initial bids for physical goods immediately fell to around 92 yuan. Preparatory transactions were made at 2.5 yuan and 3 yuan. The market situation after opening was relatively stable and could still rally. However, with bank demand exceeding supply, a decline was inevitable. The HSBC Bank announced its exchange rates for British and American currencies, which remained unchanged. At this time, the situation was most stable. Later, the exchange market was flat before rebounding. However, with differing sentiments and high-selling activity in the market, it soon faced setbacks again. Bank demand remained tight, and the gold market gradually softened. However, the situation was extremely stable, with no unexpected changes, and transactions were not large. The trend was mostly bullish. The afternoon market was flat. A telegram from Bombay reported a decline of one anna and a "do not move" message, indicating a slight rise. However, the trend remained weak, and large traders vigorously sold off, leading to a decline. However, with normal domestic bank trading and buyers still willing to participate, coupled with bargain hunters, gold prices were maintained, and the closing was relatively stable. The fluctuations throughout the day were narrow, with both rises and falls appearing weak, mainly due to limited trading. A large amount of Tianjin goods arrived, and Eastern goods also landed, totaling about 10,000 taels of spot goods. In addition, with the maturity of public bonds approaching, the swap discount fell back to one yuan. The price of fine gold was calculated at 1004 yuan and 3 jiao, with Tianjin goods priced at an additional 13.5 yuan. The market situation for the day is recorded below.

Frightening Rise in Grain and Flour Prices 248

The flour market, after opening this morning, showed another relentless surge in prices for all months. Imported wheat was quoted at Chicago, up 90 cents to one dollar, and Canadian wheat up 50 to 60 cents. When the opening prices were announced, sentiment was already agitated, due to the urgent need for grain after the North Manchurian floods, coupled with rising prices for imported wheat. Unseasonal droughts and floods within the country, and recent nervous activity in Tianjin, all contributed to a worsening environment of demand exceeding supply. Concerns remain that the situation may further tighten. In the early trading, due to strong sales to the North, Tianjin, Dalian, Yingkou, and other northern regions showed brisk purchases, causing the market to jump by 4, 5, or 6 cents. At that time, major factories sold over 100,000 bags, but the surge barely subsided. In the second and third trading sessions, large players such as silver houses also offloaded 500,000 to 600,000 bags, seeming to calm the market slightly. However, as northern purchases remained strong, short sellers rushed to cover, causing market sentiment to rise again. With no major sellers continuing to offer, it was impossible to lower buying interest, and the market entered a surging phase. It is said that major players released over one million bags, but the market continued to soar, demonstrating the severity of the situation. Total daily trading reached 2.6 million bags, reportedly a recent record. As a result, this month's prices surged by 7.5 cents, August to October each rose by 8 cents, November rose by 7.75 cents, and December rose by 9 cents.

The wheat market, after opening this morning, showed a uniform surge in prices for all months. Imported wheat was quoted at Chicago, up 90 cents to one dollar, and Canadian wheat up 50 to 60 cents. At a time when sentiment was already favorable, the rise in imported wheat gave a further boost, and sentiment became even more frantic. Quotations from production areas in Jiangsu and Zhejiang were being snapped up by dealers and traders, and prices had already risen sharply. Around the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, prices had reached about $5.50 per bag, resulting in strong buying interest and a steadily rising market. However, the abundance of the wheat crop is generally acknowledged by both public and private sectors. The problem lies with the tight market, causing deliveries to be scattered and irregular. As a result, August rose by 6 cents, September rose by 8 cents, October and November each rose by 10 cents, and December rose by 12 cents. Current spot wheat prices have jumped 7 or 8 cents due to the surge in flour and wheat futures. Prices are: Nan-Suzhou, Wuhe, and Bengbu wheat at $3.48, Xuzhou and Shandong wheat at $3.50, Gaoyou and Daqiao wheat at $3.40, Mingguang wheat at $3.45-3.46, Huangqiao wheat at $3.43, Pukou wheat at $3.43, Yangzhou wheat at $3.24, down to $3.21. Fuxin sold 12,000 bags, and Xinda sold 6,000 bags.

Government Loan of Wheat Should Be Made Public to Ease Flour and Wheat Fever 249

The flour and wheat market has now entered a frenzied state, defying reason. Initially, the price surge was triggered by drought in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, severely impacting the autumn harvest. Rice prices rose due to the weather, and the flour and wheat markets were shaken. Subsequently, when rain fell, the market seemed to ease. However, the North Manchurian floods raised concerns about the loss of autumn grain there, and grain from within the country had to supply the Northeast. Northern purchases thus became inevitable. In recent days, rumors have spread that the government is lending flour, which is about to be imported, priced at $2.55. It is said that 1.4 million bags are being shipped in August, with 400,000 bags each for Tianjin, Shanghai, and Xiamen, and the remaining 200,000 bags to be distributed elsewhere. At a time of tight market conditions, this large-scale aid provides some relief, and the government's concern for the people's suffering will become evident to the world. However, recent rumors in the market claim that this loan of flour has already been purchased in advance by powerful individuals. At a time of intense pressure and dire food shortages, this is utterly unreasonable. The severity of the current situation is no less than the extraordinary measures taken during the great flood of 1931. Fortunately, there is a global surplus, with the government lending flour and wheat, and manufacturers actively ordering imported wheat. The public, after difficulties, should not face widespread starvation. Now, the situation is different from the past. Foreign countries are experiencing famine, and China, which lacks statistics, has a wheat crop that should be more than sufficient to cope. However, manipulation by human desires is preventing the price surge from being stopped. If this batch of loan flour can be made public for relief purposes, then the trend will be like the stabilization of imported wheat prices, which immediately calms the market. This kind of relief is something that the authorities should consider.

Silk and Tea; Overseas Silk Prices Continue to Fall 255

Waste Silk Sales to Germany Halted. Wild silk cocoons and waste materials produced in provinces such as Sichuan and Hubei, including *ti hu*, *wan hu*, *jin zi*, and *xian wei ba* (generally referred to as waste silk by customs), were traditionally sold to Germany. Foreign firms in Shanghai such as Friedemer and Meishishi shipped several hundred pieces to German territories each month. Affected by the Austrian political upheaval, German silk exports have become sluggish, and waste silk shipments to Germany have completely stopped. Recently, two German mail ships, Rheinland and others, have departed without any waste silk bound for German territories.

New Sichuan and Hubei Silk Shipments to Shanghai Scarce. Factory silk and coarse silk produced in Sichuan and Hubei provinces were popular among foreign merchants. Recently, due to repeated declines in overseas silk prices, the cost of new Sichuan and Hubei silk is not low, and European merchants in Shanghai are offering extremely low prices, making sales difficult. Therefore, shipments to Shanghai are scarce. Since the beginning of summer, imports by river steamers have been very limited. New Sichuan and Hubei silk shipments to Shanghai are limited to small postal packages of yellow factory silk delivered by the postal service daily.

Shanghai Silk Sales Stagnant. In overseas markets, silk factories remain sluggish, and the price decline has not stopped. Morning telegrams of Shanghai silk being auctioned off to European and American markets were not seen yesterday. European merchants and silk shops are still suppressing prices and purchasing cautiously, while Chinese silk merchants are finding it difficult to sell and are preparing to suspend operations and wait for an opportune time. The market is quiet, with no transactions reported.

Prices for other goods are also firm, with no fluctuations. Transactions are sporadic. Since the large-scale import of Japanese goods, sales have not been strong. 120 and 150 denier goods have followed Italian goods and are extremely firm.
